prayoge puruṣahitaṃ yajñasya ca jñāne
taṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
sarvārthaṃ dharmaṃ prathamam
upavādān anuvadet
brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyarathakārāṇāṃ yajñāḥ
niṣādasthapater iṣṭyagnyādheyam
adhvaryur yajurvedena karoty ṛgvedena hotā sāmavedenodgātā sarvair brahmā
uccair ṛgvedasāmavedābhyām upāṃśu yajuṣoccaiḥ saṃpraiṣaiḥ
saṃsvāraikasvaryam iti śabdanyāyaḥ
prāṅmukhaḥ karma kuryād ā caturthāt karmaṇaḥ prasaṃpaśyan
uttarata upacāro vihāraḥ
na yajñāṅgenātmānam abhivipariharet
na vihārād apaparyāvarteta
antarāṇi yajñāṅgāni bāhyāḥ kartāraḥ
kartṝṇāṃ ca pradhānakāriṇo 'bhyantarā bāhyā itare
yajñopavītī karmāṇi kuryāt prācīnāvītī pitryāṇy ācāntodako 'hasan
mantrāntena karma saṃnipātayet
uttaramantrasyādinā pūrvasyāntaṃ vidyāt
pūrvāmnānād aṅgānām ānupūrvyaṃ pūrvaprakaraṇaṃ codanāc cāniyamaḥ kratūnām
ghṛtam ājyaśabdena pratīyate bhāryā patnī juhūḥ āhavanīya iti home
hiraṇyaṃ jātarūpam
gārhapatye haviḥśrapaṇaṃ pratitarpaṇaṃ ca
dakṣiṇāgner ekolmukāharaṇam
brāhmaṇā ṛtvija ārṣeyā mahānto yuvāno bahvapatyāḥ
juhotīti darvihomacodanā
ājyasyādhiśrayaṇaṃ gārhapatye
paryagnikaraṇam utpavanaṃ sruksruvasaṃmārgaḥ paristaraṇaṃ paryukṣaṇam āhavanīyasyeti
tūṣṇīkāṃ darvihomadharmaḥ
āsīno juhuyāj jānvakno nigadya svāhākārāntam
jamadagnīnāṃ pañcāvattaṃ caturavattam anyeṣām
āmantrya jāmadagnyam ajāmadagnyaḥ pañcāvattī syāt
māṃsasaṃhitābhyām aṅgulībhyām aṅguṣṭhena ca puroḍāśasyāvadyet sruveṇājyapayasor mekṣaṇena caroḥ svadhitinā paśor darvyā somasya
yathādiṣṭaṃ havirbhir devatā yajaty ājyenetarāḥ
dhrauvasyājyārthān kurvīta
ājyasyopastīrya haviṣo 'vadānam abhighāraṇaṃ ca
avadāyāvadāya havirdhruvāṃ pratyabhighārayed ā sviṣṭakṛdavadānāt
ājyasthālyā dhruvām
aṅguṣṭhaparvamātrāṇy avadānāni
bhūyaḥ sviṣṭakṛte bhūyiṣṭham iḍāyāḥ
madhyād avadāya haviṣaḥ pūrvārdhād dvitīyam avadyec caturavadānasya paścārdhāt tṛtīyaṃ pañcāvadānasya
pūrvārdhāt prathamaṃ jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhineyasya gataśriyo vā
aparaṃ kaniṣṭhasya kāniṣṭhineyasya bubhūṣato vā
sarveṣāṃ haviṣāṃ sviṣṭakṛte samavadyed uttarārdhāt sakṛt sakṛc caturavadānasya dvir dviḥ pañcāvadānasya
dvir abhighārayet
yatra yājyās tatrāśrutapratyāśrute ca caturavattapañcāvatte ca
dakṣiṇena dakṣiṇātikrāmet savyenodaṅ
avadāya grahaṃ vā gṛhītvā dakṣiṇātikrāman saṃpreṣyaty amuṣmā anubrūhīti yathādevataṃ saṃpraiṣayājyayoś ca
anuvācya vāgyato bhavaty āśrāvaṇāt
āśrute cāgnīdhra ā pratyāśrāvaṇāt
pratyāśrute cādhvaryur ā yaja yajeti brūyāt
anuvākyānte praṇavaṃ dadhāti hotā
tam adhvaryuḥ praṇavenopasaṃdadhāti
o śrāvayety adhvaryur astu śrauṣaḍ ity āgnīdhraḥ pratyāśrāvayaty uttaratas tiṣṭhan sphyaṃ cedhmasaṃnahanāni codyamya
amuṣmai preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati yājyāvat svāhavanīyapradhānasthāneṣu paśusomayor amuṃ yajety ārāt
yājyānuvākyāvanti pradhānāny ājyabhāgādīni sviṣṭakṛdantāni patnīsaṃyājeṣu vājine ca
dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhiṃ pratyavasthāya vaṣaṭkārānte pārśvenāpidadhad ivānāsekaṃ haviṣo 'prakṣiṇan juhoti
mukhenāsekaṃ haviṣo vyṛṣan yaṃ dviṣyāt tam āhutiṣu hūyamānāsu manasā dhyāyet
yājyāvat svāhavanīyapradhāneṣv oṃkāre ca dakṣiṇātikramaṇam
upabhṛtam adhastād upayamya pracarati vedam upayāmam anyatra daśāṃ some
samānaṃ darśapūrṇamāsayor vidhānam anyatra nirdeśāt
ubhayatrāgneyaḥ puroḍāśaḥ
agnīṣomīyo dvitīyaḥ paurṇamāsyām aindrāgno 'māvāsyāyām asaṃnayataḥ
sāṃnāyyena samānadevataḥ
saṃnayata aindraṃ sāṃnāyyaṃ māhendraṃ vā
agnīṣomīya upāṃśuyājaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ vaiṣṇavo 'māvāsyāyām
etad ijyāpradhānam
tadaṅgānītarāṇi
arthakāraṇād dharmān āvartayed vacanād vā
somejyāgniṣṭome pradhānam
darśapūrṇamāsikānāṃ pradhānānām iṣṭipaśubandhe codanā
somasyaikāhāhīnasattreṣv aṅgānāṃ ca samanvayaḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñavarjam
pratyāmnāyapratiṣedhārthalopair aṅgānivṛttiḥ sāmānyād arthāt svāśrutyād iti
dharmaviniyoge 'nāmnāte yathārthaṃ mantrān saṃnamayet
dravyālābhe tulyārthānāṃ yathāsadṛśaṃ pratinidadhyād yathārtham atulyārthe
pradhānānāṃ dharmavipratiṣedhe bhūyastve na dharmān viniyacchet tulyāṃ pūrvacodanayā
karmaṇāṃ gaṇādeśe pratyṛcaṃ karoti pratiparyāyaṃ ca
amuṣmai praṇīyamānāyānubrūhīty ukte triruktāṃ karoti
some krīte havirdhānapravartane ca
darbhāḥ paristaraṇe
svāhākārāntāḥ samidhaḥ
agniṃ sādayiṣyann uddhatya lakṣaṇam adbhir avokṣya sādayati
saṃtatakarmasu purastād ārambhaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ prāgapavargāṇy udag vā karoti
prasavyaṃ pitryāṇi
maṅgalāni lokataḥ
karmābhyāvṛttau kṛtasaṃkhyeṣu mantrān āvartayet
saṃpraiṣānuvacaneṣv āśrutapratyāśruteṣu ca mandrasvāraḥ
sāmidhenīprabhṛtyājyabhāgānteṣūrdhvam ājyabhāgābhyām ānuyājebhyo madhyamāḥ
anuyājaprabhṛty uccair ā śaṃyvantāt
triṃśadvarṣāṇi darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajeta yāvajjīvaṃ vā
pañcadaśa dākṣāyaṇayajñena darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ sthāne
yāvajjīvam agnihotram
aniyamo 'nyatra
candrādarśanenāmāvāsyām upavaset sampūrṇena paurṇamāsīṃ pūrve vā
keśaśmaśru vāpayitvā māṃsamāṣalavaṇavarjam aśnīto yajamānaḥ patnī cāsuhitau
agniṃ gṛhṇāmi surathaṃ yo mayobhūr ya udyantam ārohati svarvideti
ādityaṃ tejasāṃ teja uttamaṃ śvoyajñāya camatāṃ devatābhyaḥ
imām ūrjaṃ pañcadaśīṃ yāḥ praviṣṭās tā devatāḥ parigṛhṇāmi sarvāḥ
paurṇamāsaṃ havir idaṃ juṣantām āmāvāsyaṃ havir idaṃ juṣantām
iti yathārūpaṃ gārhapatyād āhavanīyaṃ jvalantaṃ praṇīya mamāgne varco vihaveṣv ity anvādadhāti
uttarābhyāṃ vaihavībhyām aparayor anvavadhāya vratam upaiti
payasvatīr oṣadhayaḥ payasvad vīrudhāṃ payaḥ
apāṃ payaso yat payas tena mām indra saṃsṛja
iti pāṇī prakṣālyāgne vratapata ity āhavanīyaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate
samrāḍ asi vratapā asi vratapatir asi vrataṃ cariṣyāmi tat te bravīmi tanme gopāya tacchakeyaṃ tena śakeyaṃ tena rādhyāsam ity ādityam
yady astamitaḥ syād āhavanīyam
purastād barhirāharaṇasya paurṇamāsyāṃ vratam upeyād vatsāpākaraṇasyāmāvāsyāyām
ubhayoḥ pūrvedyuḥ samanvādhānam
nānṛtaṃ vaden na māṃsaṃ prāśnīyān na striyamupeyāt
māṣavarjaṃ sāyam āraṇyam aśnīyāt
āraṇyahaviś cet syād udakam
āhavanīyāgāre yajamāno viharati gārhapatyāgāre patnī tayor dakṣiṇā
pratyagāśiṣo 'karmayuktā mantrā yājamānam
dakṣiṇata upacāro yajamānasyāparaḥ patnyāḥ
āmantrite praṇavam uktvā yathārtham anujñānam
yathādevatam āhutim anumantrayate yathākarmasaṃyogam ārāt
ko vaḥ praṇayatīti praṇīyamānā bhūś ca kaś ca vāk ca gauś ca vaṭ ca khaṃ ca nīś ca pūś caikākṣarāḥ pūr daśamā virājo yā idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ vyānaśus tā no devīs tarasā saṃvidānāḥ svasti yajñaṃ nayata prajānatīr iti
brahmapūtāḥ stheti sādane ca
agniṃ hotāram iti havirnirvapaṇam abhimṛśen nirupyamāṇe vā japet
purastāt stambayajuṣo 'ntarvedy upaviśya
ayaṃ vedaḥ pṛthivīm anvavindad guhāhitāṃ nihitāṃ gahvareṣu
sa mahyaṃ lokaṃ yajamānāya vindatv acchidraṃ yajñaṃ bhūriretāḥ kṛṇotu
iti vedam ādatte
vedena vediṃ vividuḥ pṛthivyāḥ sā paprathe pṛthivī pārthivāni
garbhaṃ bibharti bhuvaneṣv antas tato yajñas tāyate viśvadānīm
iti trir vedena vedim abhimārṣṭi
ubhayatrājyāvekṣaṇam
pañcānāṃ tvā vātānām ityāntād anuvākasyājyagrahān
yunajmi tveti ca paridhiṣu paridhīyamāneṣv āhavanīyam
dhruvākaraṇam ubhayatra
mamāgne varca ity aṣṭābhir vaihavībhir havīṃṣy āsannāny abhimṛśet
caturhotrā ca paurṇamāsyāṃ prajākāmaḥ pañcahotrā cāmāvāsyāyāṃ svargakāmaḥ
cittiḥ srug iti daśahotāraṃ purastāt sāmidhenīnām
aṅgiraso māsya yajñasya prātaranuvākair avantu
samiddho agnir āhutaḥ svāhākṛtaḥ pipartu naḥ
iti samiddham
mano 'si prājāpatyaṃ manasā bhūtenāviśeti sruvāghāram
vāg asy aindrī sapatnakṣayaṇī vācā mendriyeṇāviśeti sraucam
devāḥ pitara iti pravare pravaryamāṇe
pṛthivī hoteti caturhotāraṃ purastāt prayājānām
vasantam ṛtūnāṃ prīṇāmi sa mā prītaḥ prīṇātu
vasantasyāhaṃ devayajyayā tejasvān payasvān bhūyāsam
grīṣmam ṛtūnāṃ prīṇāmi sa mā prītaḥ prīṇātu
grīṣmasyāhaṃ devayajyayendriyavān vīryavān bhūyāsam
varṣā ṛtūnāṃ prīṇāmi tā mā prītāḥ prīṇantu
varṣāṇām ahaṃ devayajyayā puṣṭimān paśumān bhūyāsam
śarad ṛtūnāṃ prīṇāmi sā mā prītā prīṇātu
śarado 'haṃ devayajyayānnavān varcasvān bhūyāsam
hemantaśiśirāv ṛtūnāṃ prīṇāmi tau mā prītau prīṇītām
hemantaśiśirayor ahaṃ devayajyayā sahasvāṃs tapasvān bhūyāsam
iti prayājān
agninā yajñaś cakṣuṣmān agner ahaṃ devayajyayā cakṣuṣā cakṣuṣmān bhūyāsam
somena yajñaś cakṣuṣmān somasyāhaṃ devayajyayā cakṣuṣā cakṣuṣmān bhūyāsam
ityājyabhāgau
agnir hoteti pañcahotāraṃ purastāddhaviṣām
agnirannādo 'gner ahaṃ devayajyayānnādo bhūyāsam
dabdhir nāmāsy adabdho 'haṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ dabheyam
ity upāṃśuyājau
agnīṣomau vṛtrahaṇā agnīṣomayor ahaṃ devayajyayā vṛtrahā bhūyāsam
indrāgnyor ahaṃ devayajyayendriyavān annādo bhūyāsam
indrasyāhaṃ devayajyayendriyavān bhūyāsam
mahendrasyāhaṃ devayajyayā jemānaṃ mahimānaṃ gameyam
ity auttaratanikān apy anumantrān adhīyeta
indrasya vaimṛdhasyāhaṃ devayajyayāsapatno bhūyāsam
indrasya trātur ahaṃ devayajyayā trātā bhūyāsam
pūṣṇo 'haṃ devayajyayā puṣṭimān paśumān bhūyāsam
sarasvatyā ahaṃ devayajyayā vācam annādyaṃ gameyam
aditer ahaṃ devayajyayā pra prajayā paśubhir janiṣīya
viśveṣāṃ devānām ahaṃ devayajyayā prāṇaiḥ sāyujyaṃ gameyam
dyāvāpṛthivyor ahaṃ devayajyayā pra janiṣīya prajayā paśubhiḥ
amuṣyāhaṃ devayajyayety anāmnāte 'bhyūhet
agniḥ sviṣṭakṛd yajñasya pratiṣṭhā tasyāhaṃ devayajyayā yajñena pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam ity agniṃ sviṣṭakṛtam
agnir mā duriṣṭāt pātu savitāghaśaṃsād yo no anti śapati tam etena jeṣam iti prāśitram avadīyamānam
iḍāyās tūṣṇīm
upahave vasīyasyehīti
cid asīty uccaiḥ
ghṛtena mā samukṣatety antam
asmāsv indra iti ca
māśiṣa iti nāmagrāhe
iḍā dhenuḥ sahavatsā na āgād ūrjaṃ duhānā payasā prapīnā
sā no annena haviṣota gobhir iḍā pinvatāṃ payasābhyasmān
itīḍām ārjane
bradhna pāhīti barhiṣi havīṃṣy āsannāny abhimṛśet
āgneyaṃ caturdhā vyuddiśet idam agnīdha idaṃ brahmaṇa idaṃ hotur idam adhvaryor iti
idaṃ yajamānasyeti yajamānabhāgam
diśāṃ kﾱptir asi diśaḥ prīṇāmi diśo mā prītā avantv iti vyuddiṣṭe dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti
dakṣiṇāgnau yajamāno mantrāntam odanaṃ paktvā dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyām āsādyābhimṛśet
iyaṃ sthāly amṛtasya pūrṇā sahasradhāra utso akṣīyamāṇaḥ
anenaudanenāti mṛtyuṃ tarāmy aham
prajāpater bhāgo 'sy ūrjasvān payasvān
akṣito 'sy akṣityai tvā
akṣito nāmāsi mā me kṣeṣṭhā ā mā gamyāḥ
prāṇāpānau me pāhi samānavyānau me pāhy udānarūpe me pāhi cakṣuḥśrotre me pāhi
ūrg asy ūrjaṃ mayi dhehi
prajāpatir ahaṃ tvayā sākṣād ṛdhyāsam iti
agreṇottaram udañcam udvāsya dakṣiṇataḥ sadbhya ṛtvigbhyaḥ parihṛtyādadhyāt
saṃ me saṃnatayaḥ saṃnamantām idhmasaṃnahane huta iti saṃmārgān āhitān
mahāhavir hoteti saptahotāraṃ purastād anuyājānām
barhiṣo 'haṃ devayajyayā prajāvān bhūyāsam
narāśaṃsasyāhaṃ devayajyayā vīryavān bhūyāsam
agniḥ sviṣṭakṛd yajñasya pratiṣṭhā tasyāhaṃ devayajyayā yajñena pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam
ity anuyājān
vājavatyā ubhayatra
sā me satyāśīr iti prastare prahriyamāṇe
vasv ihāgacchatv iti varaṃ vṛṇīte
vi te muñcāmīti paridhiṣu prahriyamāṇeṣv āhavanīyam
iṣṭo yajño bhṛgubhir iti saṃsrāvabhāgān
ado māgacchatv iti dvitīyaṃ varam ado māgamyād iti tṛtīyam
srucor vimocanam ubhayatra
patnī ca patnīsaṃyājān anumantrayate
somasyāhaṃ devayajyayā viśvaṃ reto dheṣīya
tvaṣṭur ahaṃ devayajyayā sarvāṇi rūpāṇi paśūnāṃ puṣeyam
devānāṃ patnīnām ahaṃ devayajyayā patnīr yajñasya mithunaṃ tāsām ahaṃ devayajyayā mithunena prabhūyāsam
rākāyā ahaṃ devayajyayā vīrān videyam
sinīvālyā ahaṃ devayajyayā paśūn videyam
kuhvā ahaṃ devayajyayā pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam
agnir gṛhapatir yajñasya pratiṣṭhā tasyāhaṃ devayajyayā yajñena gṛhaiḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ gameyam
ity agniṃ gṛhapatim
iḍāsmaṃ anuvastāṃ ghṛtena yasyāḥ pade punate devayantaḥ
vaiśvānarī śakvarī vāvṛdhānopa yajñam asthita vaiśvadevī
itīḍām
dakṣiṇāgnikā homā ubhayatra
yā sarasvatī veśabhagīneti mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe
prāyaścittāhutayaḥ samiṣṭayajuḥ kapālānāṃ vimocanaṃ praṇītānāṃ vimocanam ubhayatra
saṃ yajñapatir āśiṣeti yajamāno yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnāti
yadi pravaset samiṣṭayajuṣā saha juhuyāt prajāpater vibhān nāma lokas tasmai tvā dadhāni saha yajamāneneti
sāṃnāyyasya prāśnīyān nābrāhmaṇaḥ
idaṃ havir iti śṛtasya
dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti dadhnaḥ
antarvedi praṇītāsv avamṛśya mārjayanta ṛtvijo yajamānaś ca
āsicyamāna udake 'vicchinne sadasīty abhimantrya diṅmantraiḥ pratidiśaṃ vyutsicya
yad apsu te sarasvati goṣv aśveṣu yad vasu
tena me vājinīvati mukham aṅdhi sarasvati varcasā
iti mukhāni vimṛjate
samudraṃ vaḥ prahiṇomi svāṃ yonim abhigacchata
ariṣṭā asmākaṃ vīrā mā parāseci mat payo mā mā hiṃsīs tvaṃ dhanam
iti praṇītāśeṣaṃ ninīya
namaḥ kṛtāya karmaṇe akṛtāya karmaṇe namaḥ
ayāḍ yajñaṃ jātavedā antaraḥ pūrvo 'smin niṣadya
sa tvaṃ saniṃ suvimucā vimuñca dhehy asmāsu draviṇaṃ jātavedaḥ
iti
dakṣiṇata āhavanīyam upasthāya viṣṇuḥ pṛthivyāṃ vyakraṃsteti paryāyair yajamānas trīn krāmati
viṣṇur dikṣu vyakraṃstānuṣṭubhena chandaseti caturtham
svayaṃbhūr asīty ādityam upasthāya pratyapakrāmati
idam aham ābhyo digbhyo 'smād annādyād bhrātṛvyaṃ nirbhajāmi nirbhakto yaṃ dviṣmaḥ
idam aham asmād antarikṣād asmād annādyād bhrātṛvyaṃ nirbhajāmi nirbhakto yaṃ dviṣmaḥ
idam aham asyāḥ pṛthivyā asmād annādyād bhrātṛvyaṃ nirbhajāmi nirbhakto yaṃ dviṣmaḥ
iti
aganma svaḥ saṃ jyotiṣābhūmety āhavanīyam upasthāyedam aham amuṣya prāṇaṃ niveṣṭayāmīti pārṣṇyābhidakṣiṇaṃ niveṣṭayati
yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma ity abhicaran
tejo 'sīty āhavanīyam
agnā āyūṃṣi pavasa iti tisṛbhir gārhapatyam
agne gṛhapata iti ca
asā anu mā tanv iti nāmagrāhaṃ putrān anvātayate
jyotiṣe tantave tvety antarvedy upaviśya ye devā yajñahana iti yajamānas trīn atimokṣān japati
vedo 'sīti vedam ādatte
ghṛtavantaṃ kulāyinam iti stṛṇāti saṃtataṃ gārhapatyād adhy āhavanīyāt
gomaṃ agna iti prāṅ prakramya japati
agne vratapate vratam acāriṣaṃ taṃ te prāvocaṃ tad aśakaṃ tenāśakaṃ tenārātsam ity āhavanīyam
samrāḍ asi vratapā asi vratapatir asi vratam acāriṣaṃ tat te prāvocaṃ tad aśakaṃ tenāśakaṃ tenārātsam ity ādityam
yajño babhūva sa u vābabhūva sa prajajñe sa u vāvṛdhe punaḥ
sa prajānām adhipatir babhūva so asmāsu draviṇam ādadhātu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām
iti japitvā sarveṣu samidha ādhāya tena dharmeṇa paryukṣati
tantrādiṣu brahmiṣṭhaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇīte bhūpate bhuvanapate mahato bhūtasya pate brahmāṇaṃ tvā vṛṇa iti
vṛto japati deva savitar etaṃ tvā vṛṇate bṛhaspatiṃ brahmāṇaṃ tad ahaṃ manase prabravīmi mano vāce vāg gāyatryai gāyatrī triṣṭubhe triṣṭub jagatyai jagaty anuṣṭubhe 'nuṣṭup paṅktaye paṅktiḥ prajāpataye prajāpatir viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ
bṛhaspatir devānāṃ brahmāhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ bṛhaspate yajñaṃ gopāyāhaṃ bhūpatir ahaṃ bhuvanapatir ahaṃ mahato bhūtasya patiḥ
maho me 'voco yaśo me 'voco bhargo me 'vocaḥ stomaṃ me 'voco 'nnādyaṃ me 'vocaḥ prajāṃ me 'vocaḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ me 'voca iti
dakṣiṇataḥ karmāṇy anutiṣṭhet
brāhmaudanasya prāśiṣyann odanasyādāyaudanena juhoty odanaudanasya tvā saṃjuhomi svāheti
agne 'ṅgiro 'hutādyān mā pāhi sutrāmaṇis tvādadhānīti prāśnāti
darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ paristīrṇe vihāre tīrthena prapadya dakṣiṇata āhavanīyasya saṃstīrṇam abhimantrayate ahe daidhiṣavyod atas tiṣṭhāny asya sadane sīda yo 'smat pākatara iti
savyena tṛṇaṃ pracchidya pratyagdakṣiṇā nirasyati nirastaḥ parāvasuḥ pāpmaneti
idam aham arvāgvasoḥ sadane sīdāmi devena savitrā prasūta ity apaḥ spṛṣṭvopaviśati
ahaṃ bhūpatir ahaṃ bhuvanapatir ahaṃ mahato bhūtasya patiḥ
tad agnaye prabravīmi tad vāyave tat sūryāya
sūryo divo yajñaṃ pātu vāyur antarikṣād yajñapatiṃ pātv agnir māṃ pātu mānuṣam iti japati
āmantrito 'paḥ praṇeṣyantam anujānāti bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ praṇaya yajñaṃ devatā vardhaya tvaṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhe svarge loke yajamāno 'stu
saptarṣīṇāṃ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokas tatremaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānāya dhehi
devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspatiprasūtaḥ
oṃ praṇayeti
anāmantrito haviḥ prokṣiṣyantam anujānāty āmantrita uttarān parigrāhān idhmābarhiś cānāmantritaḥ sāmidhenīpravarau cāmantrita āśrāvaṇāya samidhe ca prokṣa yajñaṃ bṛhaspate parigṛhāṇa vediṃ prokṣa yajñaṃ prajāpate 'nubrūhi yajñaṃ pravṛṇīṣva yajñaṃ vācaspate vācam āśrāvayaitām āśrāvaya yajñaṃ devebhyaḥ prajāpate pratiṣṭha yajñam iti yathārūpam
devatā vardhaya tvam ity anuṣajet
vyāhṛtīḥ purastāt praṇavaṃ copariṣṭāt
anūcyamānāsu sāmidhenīṣu vācaṃ yacchet prayājānuyājeṣv ijyamāneṣu pradhāneṣu ca parihṛte prāśitra ā prasthānāt
yadi vācaṃ visṛjed idaṃ viṣṇuḥ
agnāviṣṇū
pāvakā naḥ sarasvatī
bṛhaspatiṃ havāmaha iti nigadya vācaṃ yacchati
mārjite 'greṇāhavanīyaṃ prāśitram āhriyamāṇaṃ pratīkṣate mitrasya tvā cakṣuṣā pratīkṣa iti
pratīkṣya sāvitreṇa pratigṛhyādityās tvā pṛṣṭhe sādayāmīti bhūmau pratiṣṭhāpya suparṇasya tvā garutmataś cakṣuṣāvekṣa ity avekṣyāṅguṣṭhenopamadhyamayā ca prāśnāty anupaspṛśan dantān agneṣ ṭvāsyena prāśnāmīti
brāhmaṇasyodareṇa bṛhaspater brahmaṇeti
prācīr apa utsicyācāmati satyena tvābhijigharmīti hṛdayadeśam abhimṛśati
indrasya tvā jaṭhare dadhāmīti nābhideśam
vāṅ ma āsan nasoḥ prāṇo 'kṣyoś cakṣuḥ karṇayoḥ śrotraṃ bāhvor balam ūrvor ojo 'riṣṭā viśvāṅgāni tanūr me tanvā saheti sarvāṇi gātrāṇi
āhitām anuyājasamidham anumantrayate eṣā te agne samit tayā tvaṃ vardhasva cāpyāyasva vardhiṣīmahi ca vayam ā ca pyāyiṣīmahi ca svāheti
vāsiṣṭhaḥ some brahmā
āsanneṣv agnīṣomīya ājyeṣu dakṣiṇata āhavanīyasyāntarvedi mantropaveśanaṃ prātaranuvākakāle ca
na dhiṣṇyān vyaveyāt
tīrthena prapadya prāyaścittāhutayaḥ pavamānānvārambhaṇaṃ dhiṣṇyopasthānam iti kriyeta
āmantrite stotrānujñānam bhūr bhuvaḥ svar devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspate stuta raśminā kṣayāya kṣayaṃ jinvety uttara uttaraś ca stomabhāgaḥ
stute grahopasthānakalaśopasthānāntaṃ kṛtvā sadaḥ praviśaty apareṇa dvāreṇa paścārdhena vihārasya dvārye saṃmṛśya yathāpūrve
uruṃ no lokam anuneṣi vidvāṃt svarvij jyotir abhayaṃ svasti
ṛṣvā ta indra sthavirasya bāhū upastheyāma śaraṇā bṛhantā
iti prapadya dakṣiṇato maitrāvaruṇadhiṣṇyasya mantropaveśanam
pūrveṇa dvāreṇa dakṣiṇā yathetaṃ niṣkramaṇam
visamāpte savane 'pareṇa
savanasaṃsthāsu yathāprasṛptam
stutaśastreṣv ā vaṣaṭkārād vācaṃ yacched upākṛte prātaranuvāka upāṃśvantaryāmayor homāddhomāt
sarvakāmasya darśapūrṇamāsau
vratopete yajamāne
devā gātuvido gātuṃ yajñāya vindata
manasaspatinā devena vātādyajñaḥ prayujyatām
iti japitvā śākhām āharati
śamīśākhāṃ palāśaśākhāṃ vā bahupalāśām apratiśuṣkāgrāṃ prācīm udīcīṃ vāhānām
iṣe tveti chittvā subhūtāyeti saṃnamati
imāṃ prācīm udīcīm iṣam ūrjam abhisaṃskṛtāṃ bahuparṇām aśuṣkāgrāṃ harāmi paśupām aham ity āharati
tayā sadarbhapiñjūlayā ṣaḍ vatsān apākaroti vāyavaḥ stheti
devo va ity ekaikāṃ saṃsparśayan gāḥ prakālayati
āpyāyadhvam aghnyā devebhyā indrāya bhāgam ity āpyāyati
mahendrāyeti mahendrayājinaḥ
śuddhā apaḥ suprapāṇe pibantīḥ śatam indrāya śarado duhānāḥ
rudrasya hetiḥ pari vo vṛṇaktu
iti vrajantīr anumantrayate
pūṣā vaḥ paraspā aditiḥ prertvarīpā indro vo 'dhyakṣo 'naṣṭāḥ punar eteti ca
dhruvā asminn iti yajamānaṃ prekṣate gṛhān vābhiparyāvartate
yajamānasya paśūn pāhīty agniṣṭhe 'nasy agnyagāre vā purastāt pratīcīṃ śākhām upakarṣati
asidaṃ dātraṃ paścād gārhapatyasya sāvitreṇādatte 'śvaparaśuṃ vā devasya tvetiprabhṛtinādada ity antena
goṣad asīti gārhapatyaṃ prekṣate
pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣa ity āhavanīye pratitapyorv antarikṣaṃ vīhi
preyam agād iti prāg vodag vābhipravrajya yataḥ kutaścid darbhān barhir āharati
devānāṃ pariṣūtam asīti pariṣūya viṣṇoḥ stupa iti stambaṃ gṛhītvātisṛṣṭo gavāṃ bhāga ity ekāṃ śnuṣṭiṃ dve vā visṛjati
devebhyas tvordhvabarhirbhya ity ūrdhvam unmṛjya mādho mopari parusta ṛdhyāsam iti dātram upahṛtya viśākhāni pratilunāti sāvitreṇa dāmīty antena
prathamalūnaṃ saṃnakhaṃ prastaraṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyāḥ saṃpṛcaḥ pāhīti tṛṇam antardhāya sādayati
ācchettā te mā riṣam iti prabhūtaṃ lūtvā japati
atas tvaṃ barhir ity ālavān abhimṛśati
sahasravalśā ity ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati
apaḥ spṛṣṭvāyupitā yonir iti śulbaṃ pratidhāyādityā rāsnāsīty āveṣṭayati tridhātu pañcadhātu saptadhātu vā
evaṃ dhātusaṃbharaṇāstaraṇayoḥ
susaṃbhṛtā tvā saṃbharāmīti śulbe barhiḥ saṃbharati
alubhitā yonir iti prastaram ādhāyendrāṇyāḥ saṃnahanam ity antāv abhisamāyacchati
pūṣā te granthiṃ grathnātv iti granthiṃ karoti
sa te mā sthād iti paścāt prāñcam upakarṣati
āpas tvām aśvinau tvām ṛṣayaḥ sapta māmṛjuḥ
barhiḥ sūryasya raśmibhir uṣasāṃ ketum ārabhe
ity ārabhyendrasya tvā bāhubhyām udyaccha ity udyacchati
bṛhaspater mūrdhnā harāmīti śirasy ādhāyorv antarikṣaṃ vīhīti vrajati
adityās tvā pṛṣṭhe sādayāmīti paścād āhavanīyasya paridhideśe 'nadhaḥ sādayitvā devaṃgamam ity upari nidadhāti
pālāśaṃ khādiraṃ vāṣṭādaśadārum idhmaṃ saṃnahyati trīṃś ca paridhīn sahaśalkān kārṣmaryamayān bilvapalāśakhadirarohītakodumbarāṇāṃ vā
sthaviṣṭho madhyamo varṣīyān aṇīyān dakṣiṇārdhyo hrasiṣṭho 'ṇiṣṭha uttarārdhyaḥ
yat kṛṣṇo rūpaṃ kṛtvā prāviśas tvaṃ vanaspatīn
tatas tvām ekaviṃśatidhā saṃbharāmi susaṃbhṛtā
iti saṃbhṛtya yajñāyur anusaṃcarān iti sahamūlair darbhaiḥ saṃnahyati
kṛṣṇo 'syākhareṣṭhāḥ
devapuraś carasa ṛdhyāsaṃ tvety upari nidadhāti
darbhāṇāṃ vedaṃ karoti vatsajñuṃ paśukāmasya trivṛtaṃ brahmavarcasakāmasya mūtakāryam annādyakāmasya
prasavyaṃ śulbaṃ kṛtvā vatsajñuṃ niveṣṭya vedāgre śulbaṃ nidhāya trir vedaśiraḥ saṃnahyaty uttaram uttaraṃ pradakṣiṇam
prādeśamātre śulbāt parivāsyotkare mūlāni gamayati
atraivāmāvāsyāyāṃ vediṃ karoti sarvaṃ sadyaḥ paurṇamāsyām
śākhāyā antarvedi palāśāni viśātya mūlataḥ pracchidyāntarvedi nyasyed upaveśaṃ ca kurvīta
śākhāyā darbhamayaṃ pavitraṃ karoty agranthi trivṛd avidalam
hute 'gnihotre parisamūhya paristīryottarato gārhapatyasya pātrebhyaḥ saṃstīrya dvaṃdvaṃ sāṃnāyyapātrāṇi prayunakti dohanaṃ nidāne kumbhīṃ śākhāpavitraṃ ca
barhiṣaḥ pavitre kurute samāvapracchinnaprāntau darbhau prādeśamātrau
pavitre stho vaiṣṇave ity oṣadhyā chittvā viṣṇor manasā pūte stha ity adbhis trir unmṛjya prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskurute
devo vaḥ savitotpunātv iti gāyatryā triḥ paccha utpūya devīr āpo 'greguva ity abhimantrya śundhadhvaṃ daivyāya karmaṇa iti pātrāṇi triḥ prokṣati
upasṛṣṭāṃ me prabrūtāt
vihāraṃ ca gāṃ copasṛṣṭām antareṇa mā saṃcāriṣur iti saṃpreṣyati
niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣo niṣṭaptā arātaya iti kumbhīṃ niṣṭapya vasūnāṃ pavitram asīti prāgagraṃ pavitram avadadhāti
dyaur asīty abhimantrya mātariśvano gharma ity adhiśrayati
anvārabhya vācaṃ yacchati
na riktam avasṛjati
poṣāya tveti vatsam avasṛjyamānam anumantrayate
ayakṣmā vaḥ prajayā saṃsṛjāmi rāyaspoṣeṇa bahulā bhavantv iti saṃgacchamānām
adityā rāsnāsīti nidīyamānām
ūrjasvatīr ghṛtavatpinvamānā jīvā jīvantīr upa vaḥ sademety upasannam
utsaṃ duhanti kalaśaṃ caturbilam iḍāṃ dhenuṃ madhumatīṃ svastaye
tad indrāgnī jinvatāṃ sūnṛtāvat tad yajamānam api svarge loke dadhātu
iti dhārāghoṣam
dogdhāraṃ pṛcchati kāmadhukṣa iti
amūm iti nāmādiśati
sā viśvāyur astv asāv iti nāmagrāham anumantrayate
sā viśvabhūr iti dvitīyām
sā viśvakarmeti tṛtīyām
dugdham avanayati
tisro yajuṣā dohayati tisras tūṣṇīm
tisṛṣu dugdhāsu trir uccair vācaṃ visṛjate
bahu dugdhīndrāya devebhyo havir iti saṃpreṣyati
mahendrāyeti mahendrayājinaḥ
visṛṣṭavāg ananvārabhyottarā dohayati
saṃpṛcyadhvam ṛtāvarīr ūrmiṇā madhumattamāḥ
pṛñcatīḥ payasā payo mandrā dhanasya sātaye
iti kumbhyāṃ saṃkṣālanam ānayati
hutaḥ stoka iti skannaprāyaścittaṃ japati
vartma kurvann udag udvāsayati dṛṃha gā dṛṃha gopatiṃ mā te yajñapatī riṣad iti
śītabudhnaṃ dadhnātanakti dvayor ekasyā vā dugdhena pūrvedyur nihitena
indrāya tvā bhāgaṃ somenātanacmīty ātanakti
mahendrāyeti mahendrayājinaḥ
yavāgūr agnihotram
tasyāḥ piṇḍaṃ pratinayaty adas tamasi viṣṇave tveti
viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣasveti nidhāyāpo jāgṛteti sodakena pātreṇāmṛnmayenāpidadhyāt
yadi mṛnmayaṃ syāt tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ vāvadadhyāt
tena dharmeṇa prātardohāya vatsān apākaroti
somayājino 'māvāsyāyāṃ nityaṃ saṃnayanaṃ yathākāmy asomayājinaḥ
śuśruvān grāmaṇī rājanya iti gataśriyaḥ
aurvo gautamo bhāradvāja iti mahendraṃ yajeran gataśriyaś ca
itare saṃvatsaram indram iṣṭvāgnaye vratapataye 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirupya mahendraṃ yajeran
amāvāsyāyām aparāhṇe piṇḍapitṛyajñāya prāgdakṣiṇaikolmukaṃ praṇayet
apeto yantv asurāḥ pitṛrūpā ye rūpāṇi pratimucyācaranti
parāpuro nipuro ye bharanty agniṣ ṭān lokāt praṇudātv asmāt
iti
uttarataḥ praṇītasya vedim uddhanti sphyena sakṛt parācīnam apeto yantv asurā ye pitṛṣada iti
prāgdakṣiṇāgrair dakṣiṇāgniṃ paristīrya dakṣiṇato 'gner ekaikaṃ pātrāṇi prayunakti caruṃ mekṣaṇaṃ piṇḍanidhānam ulūkhalamusalaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ śūrpam
sakṛd ācchinnasya barhiṣa ekapavitraṃ kṛtvā tūṣṇīṃ prokṣaṇīṃ saṃskṛtya pātrāṇi sakṛt prokṣati
ekapavitram antardhāyāgniṣṭhād adhi caruṇā vrīhīn nirvapati pūrayitvā nimṛjya kṛṣṇājine 'dhyavahanti prāgdakṣiṇamukhā parāpāvam
sakṛt phalīkṛtān dakṣiṇāgnau śrapayati prasavyam udāyāvaṃ jīvataṇḍulam
śṛtaṃ pratinayati
ghṛtenānutpūtena navanītena votpūtena śṛtam abhighārya dakṣiṇata udvāsyaikasphyāyām āsicya sakṛd ācchinnaṃ prokṣati
ekasphyām āstīrya caruṃ mekṣaṇaṃ piṇḍanidhānam ity ekaikaṃ barhiṣy āsādayati
pariśrayaty ādityasakāśāt
kaśipuṃ sopadhānaṃ paścād agner āstīrya pitṝn āvāhayati eta pitara iti
yajñopavītī mekṣaṇena tisra āhutīr juhoti
somāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ
yamāyāṅgirasvate svadhā namaḥ
agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā nama iti dakṣiṇāṃ dakṣiṇām
udakalepaṃ mekṣaṇam agnāv anupraharati
yajamāno 'ta ūrdhvaṃ paretana pitara iti trir apaḥ pariṣiñcati triḥ pātraṃ pratipariharati
trīn udakāñjalīn ninayati ācāmantu pitara iti
barhiṣi trīn piṇḍān nidadhāti dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇam etat te mama pitar asāv iti pitur nāma gṛhītvaitat te mama pitāmahāsāv iti pitāmahasyaitat te prapitāmahāsāv iti prapitāmahasya
ye cātra tvām anu tebhyaḥ svadhety anuṣajet
etat te 'muṣya pitar etat te 'muṣya pitāmahaitat te 'muṣya prapitāmaheti pravasati yajamāne 'dhvaryuḥ
yadi nāmāni na jānīyāt svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthivīṣadbhyaḥ svadhā pitṛbhyo 'ntarikṣasadbhyaḥ svadhā pitṛbhyo diviṣadbhya iti nidadhyāt
lupyeta jīvatpituḥ piṇḍanidhānam
na jīvantam atidadyāt
jīvatpitāmahaś cet pitur ekaḥ piṇḍaḥ
lepaḥ pitre
tathodakam āñjanābhyañjane ca
barhiṣi lepaṃ nimārṣṭi yātra pitaraḥ svadhā tayā yūyaṃ yathābhāgaṃ mādayadhvam iti
atra pitaro mādayadhvam ity udaṅṅ āvṛtyā tamitor āsitvā yeha pitara ūrk tasyai vayaṃ jyog jīvanto bhūyāsmety amīmadanta pitara iti pariśritaṃ prapadyāñjanāktāḥ śalākāḥ pratipiṇḍaṃ nidadhāti āṅkṣvāsāv ity āñjanenābhyaṅkṣvāsāv ity abhyañjanena ca
eṣā yuṣmākaṃ pitara ity ūrṇāṃ daśāṃ vā nyasyati
imā asmākam ity avaśiṣṭā avekṣate
lomottaravayasi nyasyed ato naḥ pitaro 'nyan mā yoṣṭeti
tena dharmeṇa pariṣicya mārjayantāṃ pitaro mārjayantāṃ pitāmahā mārjayantāṃ prapitāmahā iti barhiṣi trīn udakāñjalīn ninīya nihnute 'ñjaliṃ kṛtvā namo vaḥ pitaro manyave
namo vaḥ pitara iṣe
namo vaḥ pitara ūrje
namo vaḥ pitaraḥ śuṣmāya
namo vaḥ pitaro rasāya
namo vaḥ pitaro balāya
namo vaḥ pitaro yajjīvaṃ tasmai
namo vaḥ pitaro yad ghoraṃ tasmai
svadhā vaḥ pitaro namo namo vaḥ pitaraḥ
ye 'tra pitaraḥ pretā yuṣmāṃs te 'nu ya iha pitaro jīvā asmāṃs te 'nu
ye 'tra pitaraḥ pretā yūyaṃ teṣāṃ vasiṣṭhā bhūyāstha ya iha pitaro jīvā ahaṃ teṣāṃ vasiṣṭho bhūyāsam iti
śeṣam avajighret
āmayāvy annādyakāmo vā prāśnīyāt
prajāpate na tvad ity uttiṣṭhati
paretaneti yajamānaḥ pravāhaṇīṃ japati
ubhau manasvatīr mano nvāhuvāmaha iti tisraḥ
vayaṃ soma vrate tava manas tanūṣu bibhrataḥ
prajāvantaḥ sacemahi
iti ca
akṣann amīmadanteti ca
prāpyā te agna idhīmahīti gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate
madhyamaṃ piṇḍaṃ patnī prāśnīyāt
ādhatta pitaro garbhaṃ kumāraṃ puṣkarasrajam
yathāyaṃ pumān syāt
iti
itarāv agnāv anuprahared brāhmaṇo vāśnīyād apo vā gamayet
dve dve abhyukṣya pātrāṇi pratyāharati
aupāsanaṃ gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnisthānīyaṃ kṛtvāpyanāhitāgniḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñaṃ kurvīta
prātarhute 'gnihotre veṣāya vām iti pāṇī prakṣālyāgnīn paristīrya dakṣiṇato brahmayajamānābhyāṃ stīrtvā saṃtataṃ pṛṣṭhyāṃ stṛṇāti gārhapatyād adhy āhavanīyād yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatyai stṛṇāmīti
uttarataḥ pṛṣṭhyāyāḥ pātrebhyaḥ saṃstīrya dvaṃdvaṃ pātrāṇi prayuṇakti sphyaṃ kapālāny agnihotrahavaṇīṃ śūrpaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ śamyām ulūkhalamusalaṃ dṛṣadupalaṃ khādiraṃ sruvaṃ pālāśīṃ juhūm āśvatthīm upabhṛtaṃ vaikaṅkatīṃ dhruvāṃ śamīmayīr vāratnimātrīḥ
varaṇamayāni śiṣṭāni pātrāṇi
pātrīm iḍācamasaṃ vedaṃ vedapraravān kuṭarum ājyasthālīṃ caruṃ prāśitraharaṇaṃ praṇītāpātraṃ patnīyoktraṃ prātardauhikāni
camasenāpaḥ praṇayati
kāṃsyena brahmavarcasakāmasya dohanena paśukāmasya mṛnmayena pratiṣṭhākāmasyāyasenābhicarataḥ
vānaspatyo 'sīti camasam ādāya devebhyaḥ śundhasveti camasaṃ prakṣālayati
pārthivam asi
devebhyaḥ śumbhasvetītarān
paścād gārhapatyasya pavitrāntarāpo gṛhṇīte pṛthivīṃ manasā dhyāyan
yad vo revatī revatyaṃ yad vo haviṣyā haviṣyam
yad va ojo yac ca nṛmṇaṃ taṃ va ūrmiṃ madhumantaṃ devayajyāyai juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmi
iti
prokṣaṇīr dharmaiḥ saṃskṛtya brahmann apaḥ praṇeṣyāmīty āmantryāvadhāya pavitre sphyena saha praṇayati samaṃ prāṇair dhārayamāṇaḥ ko vaḥ praṇayati sa vaḥ praṇayatu
kasmai vaḥ praṇayati tasmai vaḥ praṇayatu
bṛhaspatir vaḥ praṇayatu
poṣāya tveti
uttarata āhavanīyasya sphyenoddhatya sādayati ko vo yunakti sa vo yunaktu
kasmai vo yunakti tasmai vo yunaktu
bṛhaspatir vo yunaktu
viśvebhyaḥ kāmebhyo devayajyāyā iti
adhvaryuyajamānau vācaṃ yacchetām ā haviṣkṛtaḥ
paristaraṇaiḥ svācchādya pavitrapāṇiḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati saṃsīdantāṃ daivīr viśa iti
vānaspatyāsīty agnihotrahavaṇīm ādatte
varṣavṛddham asīti śūrpam
urv antarikṣaṃ vīhīti vrajati
pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣa ity āhavanīye pratitapya yajamāna havir nirvapsyāmīti yajamānam āmantrayate
yadi pravased agne nirvapsyāmīti brūyāt
vrīhyāgrayaṇeneṣṭvā vrīhibhir yajetā yavebhyo yavair vā vrīhibhyaḥ
paścād agniṣṭhaṃ śakaṭaṃ yogyakṛtaṃ chadiṣmat sapariṇaṭkam
tasmād adhi nirvapati
pātryā vā sphyam avadhāyānasān mantrān japan
dhūr asīti dhuram abhimṛśati
devānām asi vahnitamam ity uttarām īṣām ālabhya japati
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīti pādam ādadhāti
ahrutam asīty ārohati
uru vātāyety avasārayati
mitrasya vaś cakṣuṣā prekṣa iti haviṣyān prekṣate
agnihotrahavaṇyām avadhāya muṣṭinā nirvapaty agnihotrahavaṇyāḥ śūrpe devasya va ity agnaye vo juṣṭān nirvapāmy amuṣmai vo juṣṭān iti yathādevatam
trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
idaṃ devānām iti niruptān abhimṛśati
idam u naḥ sahety avaśiṣṭān
gopīthāya tvā rakṣāyai tvā nārātyā iti niruptān
dṛṃhantāṃ duryā ity avarohati
svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti skannaprāyaścittaṃ japati
nirvaruṇasyeti śakaṭaṃ niṣkrāmayati
svar abhivyakśam ity ākāśaṃ prekṣate
jyotir vaiśvānaram ity āhavanīyam
urv antarikṣam anvihi
adityāstvopasthe sādayāmīti paścād gārhapatyasya sādayati
agne havyaṃ rakṣasveti pura upasādayati
anirmṛṣṭāyām agnihotrahavaṇyāṃ prokṣaṇīṃ saṃskṛtya haviṣyaṃ prokṣaty anabhiprokṣann agnim agnaye vo juṣṭān prokṣāmy amuṣmai vo juṣṭān iti yathādevatam
trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
pātrāṇi ca yad vo 'śuddha ālebha iti trir uttānāni paryāvartya
adityās tvag asīti kṛṣṇājinam ādāyāvadhūtaṃ rakṣa ity utkare trir avadhūnoty upariṣṭādgrīvam udagāśasanam
adityās tvag asi prati tvādityās tvag vettv iti
paścād utkarasyāstṛṇāti pratyaggrīvam uttaraloma pratyagbhasadam abhibhujan
anutsṛjan kṛṣṇājinam ulūkhalam ādadhāti pṛthugrāvāsīti
na riktam avasṛjati
agner jihvāsīti haviṣyān vapati
trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
bṛhadgrāvāsīti musalam ādāya
ūrdhvasūr vānaspatya iti vā
apahataṃ rakṣo haviṣkṛd ehīty avahanti
apahato 'ghaśaṃso haviṣkṛd ehīti dvitīyam
apahatā yātudhānā haviṣkṛd ehīti tṛtīyam
haviṣkṛd āgahīti rājanyasya haviṣkṛd ādraveti vaiśyasya
patny avahanti
kuṭarur asīty āgnīdhraḥ kuṭarum ādāyeṣam āvadeti dṛṣadam āhanti
ūrjam āvadeti dvitīyaṃ rāyaspoṣam āvadety upalām
trir etena dharmeṇa
varṣavṛddhamasīti śūrpam ādatte
varṣavṛddhāḥ stheti haviṣyān prekṣate
prati tvā varṣavṛddhaṃ vettv ity udvapati
parāpūtaṃ rakṣa ity uttare niṣpunāti
puroḍāśakapāle tuṣān opyādhastāt kṛṣṇājinasyopāsyati praviddho rakṣasāṃ bhāga iti
idam ahaṃ rakṣo 'vabādha idam ahaṃ rakṣo 'dhamaṃ tamo nayāmīti pārṣṇyā tuṣān avabādhate
apaḥ spṛṣṭvā vivinakti devo vaḥ savitā vivinaktu suvicā vivicyadhvam iti
viviktān āvapati
devebhyaḥ śundhadhvam iti triḥ phalīkaroti
tena dharmeṇānabhibhujan kṛṣṇājinam āstīrya dhiṣaṇāsi pārvatīti dṛṣadam ādadhāti
dhiṣaṇāsi pārvatī prati tvā pārvatī vettv ity upalām
adityāḥ skambho 'sīti śamyām upakarṣati paścādudīcīnakumbām
dhānyam asīty adhivapati trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
prāṇāya tveti prācīm upalāṃ prakarṣaty apānāya tveti pratīcīṃ vyānāya tveti madhye vyavadhārayati
dīrghām anu prasṛtim iti saṃsthāpayati
mitrasya vaś cakṣuṣāvekṣa iti piṣṭāny avekṣate
devo vaḥ savitā hiraṇyapāṇir upagṛhṇātv ity avaśīryamāṇāny upagṛhṇāti
dāsī pinaṣṭi patnī vā
aṇūni kurutād iti saṃpreṣyati
dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāya gārhapatyād aṅgārau nirvartayaty apāgne 'gnim āmādaṃ jahīti
niṣkravyādaṃ nudasvety anyataraṃ nirasyati
āgne devayajanaṃ vaheti dvitīyam avasthāpya tasmin kapālam upadadhāti dhruvam asi pṛthivīṃ dṛṃheti
anabhisṛjan kapālam aṅgāram adhivartayati nirdagdhaṃ rakṣa iti
dharuṇam asīti pūrvam upadadhāti
dhartram asīti pūrvārdham
dharmāsīti madhyamād dakṣiṇam
cid asīty uttaram
paricid asīti dakṣiṇārdhāt pūrvam
viśvāsu dikṣu sīdety aparam
sajātān asmai yajamānāya pariveśaya sajātā imaṃ yajamānaṃ pariviśantv ity uttarārdhāt pūrvam
aṣṭākapāla āgneya ekādaśakapāla aindrāgna aindraś ca
etena dharmeṇottarasminn aṣṭāv upadhāya citaḥ stha paricitaḥ stheti śeṣam upadadhāti
vasūnāṃ rudrāṇām ity aṅgārān adhyūhya taptābhyaś carum adhiśritya prātardohaṃ dohayati yathā sāyaṃdoham
udagagraṃ pavitram avadadhāti
śṛtaṃ karoti nātanakti
udvāsya prātardohaṃ piṣṭāni saṃvapati niṣṭapyopavātāyāṃ pātryāṃ pavitre avadhāya vāgyato devasya va ity agnaye juṣṭān saṃvapāmy amuṣmai vo juṣṭān iti yathādevataṃ trir yajuṣā tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
taptā apo madantīr utpūya havir utpunāti paccho gāyatryā
āharati sruveṇa praṇītānāṃ vedam upayāmaṃ kṛtvā
tābhiḥ saṃsṛjati sam āpā oṣadhībhir iti
adbhiḥ pariprajātāḥ stha sam adbhiḥ pṛcyadhvam iti madantībhiḥ
sīdantu viśa iti saṃnayati
makhasya śiro 'sīti piṇḍam abhimantrya pūṣā vāṃ viśvavedā vibhajatu yathābhāgaṃ vyāvartethām iti samau karoti
idam agner ity āgneyam idam agnīṣomayor ity abhimantrya paurṇamāsyām
yathādevatam amāvāsyāyām
gharmo 'sīty adhiśrayati
uru prathasveti prathayati yāvatkapālaṃ kūrmasyānurūpam aśvaśaphamātram
saṃ te tanvā tanvaḥ pṛcyantām ity avikṣārayan lepena parimārṣṭi
dakṣiṇata ājyaṃ nirvapati
aditir asi nāchinnapatrety ājyasthālīm ādāya dakṣiṇāgnau vilāpya pavitrāntarā pṛśneḥ payo 'sy agreguvas tasya te 'kṣīyamāṇasya pinvamānasya jinvamānasyeṣa ūrje juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi devayajyāyā iti
pari vājapatir ity ājyaṃ haviś ca triḥ paryagnikaroti saha lepena
devas tvā savitā śrapayatv ity ulmukenābhitāpyāgne brahma gṛhṇīṣvety ulmukam avasṛjya darbhais tvacaṃ grāhayaty agniṣ ṭe tvacaṃ mā hiṃsīd ity anapohan jvālān
saṃ brahmaṇā pṛcyasveti vedena sahāṅgāraṃ bhasmābhyūhati
avidahanta śrapayatety aṅgārān abhyūhya vācaṃ visṛjate
antarvedi prāgudīcīḥ sphyena tisro lekhāḥ kṛtvā tāsu lepaṃ ninayaty asaṃsārayan ekatāya svāhā dvitāya svāhā tritāya svāheti paryāyair āhavanīyād ulmukenābhitāpya
vediṃ karoti
khādiraṃ sphyaṃ bhṛṣṭilam ādatte sāvitreṇa
indrasya bāhur asīti darbheṇa saṃmṛjya pṛthivyā varmāsīti pūrvasmin veditṛtīye darbhaṃ nidhāya sphyena tiryak chinatti tricaturthaṃ pṛthivi devayajanīti
vrajaṃ gaccha gosthānam iti tṛṇāgram ādatte pāṃsūṃś cākhātvā
varṣatu te parjanya iti vedim avekṣate
badhāna deva savitar iti sphyena satṛṇān pāṃsūn harati
uttarata āgnīdhras tuṣān vedamūlānīty utkaraṃ parigṛhṇāti
idaṃ tasmai harmyaṃ karomi yo vo devāś carati brahmacaryam
medhāvī dikṣu manasā tapasvy antardūtaś carati mānuṣeṣu
iti tasya pāṇikoṣṭhe nivapati
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma ity abhicaran
mā vaḥ śivā oṣadhaya iti dvitīyam
drapsas ta iti tṛtīyam
etena dharmeṇa trir yajuṣā harati tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
apabāḍhaṃ rakṣo 'pabāḍho 'ghaśaṃso 'pabāḍhā yātudhānā iti sphyenotkaram apidhatte
agreṇa gārhapatyam apareṇāhavanīyaṃ sphyena vediṃ parigṛhṇāti yajamānamātrāṃ prācīṃ yathā havīṃṣy āsannāni sambhaveyus tāvatīṃ tiraścīm
satyasad asīti paścārdhād udīcīṃ lekhāṃ likhati
ṛtasad asīti dakṣiṇārdhāt prācīm
gharmasad asīty uttarārdhāt prācīm
kheyāṃ pratiṣṭhākāmasya kuryāt
apārarum iti dvyaṅgulaṃ khātvā sphyena mūlāny uddhatyotkare nivapati
āhāryapurīṣāṃ paśukāmasya kuryāt
imāṃ naraḥ kṛṇuta vedim etya devebhyo juṣṭām adityā upasthe
tāṃ viśve devā ajuṣanta sarve rāyaspoṣā yajamānaṃ saṃviśantu
iti saṃmṛṣṭām āhavanīyalakṣmyai prāñcāv aṃsāv unnayati pratīcī śroṇī prāgudakpravaṇāṃ saṃnatamadhyām antikajaghanām
etadantaṃ pūrvedyuḥ karoti
pāṇī prakṣālya sphyaṃ prakṣālayaty apratimṛśann agram
vedim avokṣya brahmann uttaraṃ parigrahīṣyāmīty āmantrya parigṛhṇāti vasavas tveti paścād rudrās tveti dakṣiṇata ādityās tvety uttarataḥ
dhā asi svadhā asi
urvī cāsi vasvī cāsi rantī cāsi
purā krūrasyeti ca sphyena vediṃ saṃmṛjyāparasmin veditṛtīye tiryañcaṃ sphyaṃ stabdhvā prokṣaṇīr āsādayedhmābarhir upasādaya sruvaṃ srucaś ca saṃmṛḍḍhi patnīṃ saṃnahyājyenodehīti saṃpreṣyati
āgnīdhro yathāpreṣitaṃ karoti
prokṣaṇīr abhyutpūrya sphyāgre 'pa upaninīyodañcaṃ sphyam avakṛṣya sphyasya vartman sādayati
purāsadanāt sphyam udyacchet
sphyenotkaram avahanti dviṣato vadho 'sīti purastāt pratyañcam
abhyukṣya pratyāsādayati
uttarata āhavanīyasya dakṣiṇam idhmam uttaraṃ barhiḥ
vedapraravaiḥ srucaḥ saṃmārṣṭi caturdhā vibhajyāvibhajya vā
āhavanīye gārhapatye vā pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣa iti pratitapyābhyagre sapārśvāgrair mukhāni mūlair daṇḍān
āyuḥ prāṇam iti sarvataḥ sruvam agneṣ ṭvā tejiṣṭhasya tejasā niṣṭapāmīti saṃmārgaṃ niṣṭapati
cakṣuḥ śrotram iti juhūm abhyantaraṃ prācīṃ pratīcīṃ bāhyataḥ
vācaṃ paśūn ity upabhṛtam abhyantaraṃ pratīcīṃ prācīṃ bāhyataḥ
yajñaṃ prajām iti sarvato dhruvām
abhyukṣya saṃmārgān agnāv anupraharati
divaḥ śilpam avatataṃ pṛthivyāḥ kakubhi śritam
tenā sahasrakāṇḍena dviṣantaṃ tāpayāmasi
dviṣan nas tapyatāṃ bahu mā na āgāt tāpyauṣadhayaḥ svāhā
iti
agne gṛhapata upa mā hvayasva devānāṃ patnīr upa mā hvayadhvam iti patnī gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate
patnīlokaṃ ca patni patny eṣa te loko namas te astu mā mā hiṃsīr iti
suprajasas tvā vayaṃ supatnīr upasedima
agne sapatnadambhanaṃ suvīrāso adābhyam
iti dakṣiṇataḥ paścād gārhapatyasyopaviśati prabhujya jānunī
yoktreṇa patnī saṃnahyate 'ntarvastram āśāsānā saumanasaṃ prajāṃ saubhāgyaṃ tanūm
agner anuvratā bhūtvā saṃnahye sukṛtāya kam
iti
pūṣā te granthiṃ grathnātv iti granthiṃ karoti
sa te mā syād iti dakṣiṇato granthim abhyūhati
apaḥ spṛṣṭvā vedenājyam upaharati
tad anvārabhyābhisaṃmīlyāvekṣate adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣāvekṣe rāyaspoṣāya suprajāstvāya
aditir iva suputrendrāṇīvāvidhavā suprajāḥ prajayā bhūyāsam iti
idaṃ viṣṇur iti gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyor adhiśrayati
tejo 'sīti dvitīyaṃ paścād gārhapatyasya
tejo 'nupracyavasveti harati
agneṣ ṭe haro mā vinaid ity āhavanīye 'dhiśrityottarataḥ prokṣaṇīnāṃ sphyasya vartman sādayati
tejo 'sīti paryāyais trir ājyam utpūyāpa utpunāti paccho gāyatryā
amṛtam asīty ājyam avekṣate
antarvedy ājyāni sruveṇa gṛhṇāti vedam antardhāya pavitre avadhāya dhāmāsīti gṛhṇaṃś caturjuhvāṃ gṛhṇāti
aṣṭau gṛhṇann upabhṛti kanīyaś caturdhruvāyām
bhūyiṣṭhaṃ pañcamaṃ paśukāmasya
āpo rebhata pipṛta madhvā samaktā niṣāda sthā yāmanvāhāryamāṇā iti prokṣaṇīr abhimantrayate
devīr āpaḥ śuddhā yūyam iti ca
brahmann idhmaṃ vediṃ barhiḥ prokṣiṣyāmīty āmantrya visrasyedhmamṛte paridhibhyaḥ prokṣati
kṛṣṇo 'syākhareṣṭha itīdhmaṃ vedir asīti vediṃ barhir asīti barhis tris triḥ prokṣati
devaṃgamam asīty antarvedy āsādya barhis triḥ prokṣati dive tvety agram antarikṣāya tveti madhyaṃ pṛthivyai tveti mūlam
agrāṇy upapāyya granthiṃ pariṣicya mūlāny upasiñcati
ūrg bhava barhiṣadbhyaḥ
svāhā pitṛbhyo gharmapāvabhya iti dakṣiṇato vedyāḥ prokṣaṇīśeṣaṃ ninīya pūṣā te granthiṃ viṣyatv iti granthiṃ visrasya yajamāne prāṇāpānau dadhāmīti prastare pavitre visṛjya viṣṇoḥ stupo 'sīti prastaraṃ sahapavitram āhavanīyato 'bhigṛhṇāty avidhūnvann asaṃmārgam
agreṇāhavanīyaṃ parihṛtya dakṣiṇato brahmaṇe yajamānāya vā prayacchati prāṇāpānābhyāṃ tvā satanuṃ kṛṇomīti
mayi prāṇāpānāv iti pratigṛhṇāti
darbhān antardhāya dakṣiṇataḥ śulbaṃ stṛṇāty uttaram aṃsam abhistṛṇan barhiḥstaraṇamantreṇa
paścārdhād udagagram apatnīkasya nidadhyāt
uru prathasveti staraṇam
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ dhātum aparam aparaṃ vā stṛṇāti
chādayan mūlāni prācīnam antardadhāti vedim
prastarahastaḥ paridhibhir āhavanīyaṃ paridadhāti gandharvo 'sīti paścārdhyam udañcam indrasya bāhur asīti dakṣiṇārdhyaṃ prāñcaṃ mitrāvaruṇau tvety uttarārdhyaṃ prāñcam
avakṛṣyāgrataram idhmād ūrdhve samidhāv ādadhāti nityahotāraṃ tveti
tūṣṇīm uttarām
sūryas tvā raśmibhir ity āhavanīyam upasthāya purastād apracchinnaprāntau darbhāv anantargarbhāv udagagrau barhiṣi vitanoti viśvajanasya vidhṛtī stha iti
vidhṛtyoḥ prastaraṃ sādayati dakṣiṇārdhe barhiṣaḥ vasūnāṃ rudrāṇām iti
dyaur asīti prastare juhūm
samaṃ prastaramūlair daṇḍaṃ karoti
antarikṣam asīty uttarām upabhṛtam adhastād vidhṛtyoḥ
pṛthivy asīty uttarāṃ dhruvām upariṣṭād vidhṛtyoḥ
asaṃspṛṣṭāḥ sādayaty anūcīḥ
ṛṣabho 'sīti dakṣiṇato juhvāḥ pūrṇasruvaṃ sādayati
dhruvā asadann ity ājyāni saṃmṛśati
syonaṃ te sadanaṃ kṛṇomi ghṛtasya dhārayā suśevaṃ kalpayāmīti pātryām upastīryābhighārya havīṃṣy udvāsayati
ārdraḥ pṛthasnur bhuvanasya gopāḥ śṛta utsnātu janitā matīnām iti
surūpaṃ tvā vasuvidaṃ paśūnāṃ tejasāgnaye tvā juṣṭam abhighārayāmīty āgneyam abhighārayati yathādevatam uttaram
anabhighnann aparyāvartayan vedena pramṛjya pātryām avadadhāti
irā bhūtiḥ pṛthivyā raso motkramīd iti kapālāny abhighārya puroḍāśāv alaṃkaroti
tṛptir asi gāyatraṃ chandas tarpaya mā tejasā brahmavarcasena
tṛptir asi traiṣṭubhaṃ chandas tarpaya mendriyeṇa vīryeṇa
tṛptir asi jāgataṃ chandas tarpaya mā prajayā paśubhiḥ
kham aṅkṣva tvacam aṅkṣva sarvam ātmānam aṅkṣveti svaktam anīkāśam anakti
adhastād upājya dohāv alaṃkaroti
yas ta ātmā paśuṣu praviṣṭo devānāṃ veṣṭām anu yo vicaṣṭe
ātmanvān soma ghṛtavān ihehi svar vinda yajamānāya mahyam
iti
paścātsrucāṃ pratyagdaṇḍāṃ pātrīm āsādayaty agreṇa srucaḥ kumbhyau saṃdhāya dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ śṛtam uttarasyāṃ dadhyagreṇa sruco vedaṃ sādayati
vedyantān paristīrya hotṛṣadanam āstīryāgnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
praṇave praṇave samidham ādadhāty anuyājasamidham avaśiṣya
samiddham agniṃ trir vedenopavājayaty agraṃ vedyāḥ saṃmārgam
dhruvāyāṃ pūrṇasruvam avanīya dhruvāyā upahatyottareṇa paridhisaṃdhinānvavahṛtya dakṣiṇāprāñcam āghāram āghārayati prajāpataye svāheti manasā
agnīt paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca tris triḥ saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati
sphyena saṃmārṣṭīdhmasaṃnahanaiś ca paridhīn
ṛte sphyād agnim idhmasaṃnahanaiḥ saṃmārṣṭy ājiṃ tvāgne sariṣyantaṃ saniṃ saniṣyantaṃ vājaṃ jeṣyantaṃ devebhyo havyaṃ vakṣyantaṃ vājinaṃ tvā vājajityāyai saṃmārjmi
agne vājaṃ jayeti
saprathā nama iti purastāj juhūpabhṛtor añjaliṃ karoti
juhvety agniṣ ṭvā hvayati devān yakṣyāvo devayajyayā iti juhūm ādatte
upabhṛd ehi devas tvā savitā hvayati devān yakṣyāvo devayajyayā ity upabhṛtam
suyame me adya stam ity abhimantryāgnāviṣṇū ity atikrāmati
viṣṇoḥ sthāmāsīty avatiṣṭhate
antarvedi dakṣiṇaḥ pādo bhavaty avaghra iva savyaḥ
athāghāram āghārayati ūrdhvo adhvara iti prāgudañcaṃ saṃtatam ūrdhvaṃ svargakāmasya nyañcaṃ dveṣyasya
asaṃsparśayan srucau pratyatikrāmati pāhi māgne duścaritād ā mā sucaritād bhajeti
juhvā dhruvāṃ triḥ samanakti
samaktam agninā haviḥ samaktaṃ haviṣā ghṛtam
sam antarikṣam arciṣā saṃ jyotiṣā jyotiḥ
iti
dhruvām abhighāryāyatane srucau sādayati
unnītaṃ rāya iti dhruvāyā ājyam unnayati suvīrāya svāheti juhūm āpyāyayati
yajñena yajñaḥ saṃtata iti juhvā dhruvāṃ pratyabhighārayati
uttarataḥ pravarāyāvatiṣṭhate
sphyasaṃmārgaṃ pāṇau kṛtvāpara āgnīdhro vedyās tṛṇam avyantam apādāyāha ka idam adhvaryur bhaviṣyati sa idam adhvaryur bhaviṣyati
yajño yajñasya
viṣṇoḥ sthāne tiṣṭhāmi
vāg ārtvijyaṃ karotu mana ārtvijyaṃ karotu
vācaṃ prapadye
bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ
brahman pravarāyāśrāvayiṣyāmīty āmantryāśrāvya pratyāśruta āha agnir devo daivyo hotā devān yakṣad vidvāṃś cikitvān manuṣvad bharatavad amuvad amuvad iti
ūrdhvān ṛṣīn mantrakṛto yajamānasya pravṛṇīte
purohitapravarenābrāhmaṇasya
brahmaṇvad ā ca vakṣad brāhmaṇā asya yajñasya prāvitāra iti
hotur upāṃśu nāmādiśati mānuṣa ity uccaiḥ
ghṛtavatīti saṃpreṣyati
srucāv ādāya samidho yajeti prathame saṃpreṣyati yaja yajety uttarān
trīn iṣṭvopabhṛto 'rdhaṃ juhvām ānīyottarau yajati
pañca prayājān uttareṇāghārasaṃbhedaṃ samānatra yajati
dhruvādīni havīṃṣy abhighārayaty upabhṛtam antataḥ
jyotiṣmatyājyabhāgau yajaty āgneyam uttarārdhe saumyaṃ dakṣiṇārdhe 'greṇāghārasaṃbhedam atikrāmam
pradhānāhutīḥ pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ saṃhitām
āgneyena pracaryopāṃśuyajñena pracarati
upāṃśu devatām āhoccair anyat
sāṃnāyyena samānadevatasya dohayoś ca samavadāya pracarati
purastāt sviṣṭakṛtaḥ sruvena pārvaṇau homau juhoti
ṛṣabhaṃ vājinaṃ vayaṃ pūrṇamāsaṃ havāmahe
sa no dohatāṃ suvīraṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇam
pūrṇamāsāya surādhase svāheti paurṇamāsyām
amāvāsyā subhagā suśevā dhenur iva payo bhūya āpyāyamānā
sā no dohatāṃ suvīraṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇam
amāvāsyāyai surādhase svāhā
ity amāvāsyāyām
uttarārdhapūrvārdhe 'gniṃ sviṣṭakṛtam asaṃsṛjan yajati
āyatane srucau sādayati
āgneyamadhyād adhihatyāṅguṣṭhenopamadhyamayā ca yavamātraṃ prāśitram avadyati
anupastṛṇann abhighāryāgreṇottaraṃ vedyaṃsam apa upaninīya vyūhyauṣadhīḥ sādayati
sarveṣāṃ haviṣāṃ dvir dvir iḍāṃ samavadāya sādayati
āgneyasya dakṣiṇārdhād avadāya pūrvārdhād aṇuṃ dīrghaṃ yajamānabhāgam avadyati
madhyāt sambhindan dvitīyām iḍām
agreṇa havīṃṣi paścārdhena srucaḥ parihṛtya pratyaṅmukha āsīno hotra iḍāṃ prayacchati
agreṇa hotāram apareṇeḍāṃ dakṣiṇātikramyānatikramya vā hotur aṅguliparvaṇī anakty aparaṃ pūrvam
iḍāyā hotre 'vāntareḍāṃ haste 'vadyati hotā pūrvam adhvaryur uttaram
adhvaryur āgnīdhro brahmayajamānāv ity anvārabhante
upahūtāyām iḍāyāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ parītottarataḥ parīteti saṃpreṣyati
yajamānapañcamā ṛtvijo vyatikramya bhakṣayitveḍāṃ prastare mārjayante
mano jyotir juṣatām ājyasya vicchinnaṃ yajñaṃ sam imaṃ dadhātu
bṛhaspatis tanutām imaṃ no yajñaṃ viśve devā iha mādayantām
iti
vyuddiṣṭasya dvaidham āgnīdhrabhāgaṃ pṛthak pāṇyor avadyaty upahūtā pṛthivī mātopa māṃ pṛthivī mātā hvayatām agnir āgnīdhrāt svāhā
upahūto dyauḥ pitopa māṃ dyauḥ pitā hvayatām agnir āgnīdhrāt svāhety upahūya pṛthivyās tvā dātrā prāśnāmy antarikṣasya tvā dātrā prāśnāmi divas tvā dātrā prāśnāmi diśāṃ tvā dātrā prāśnāmīti prāśnāti
vedena brahmabhāgayajamānabhāgāv agreṇāhavanīyaṃ parihṛtya dakṣiṇataḥ prāśitraharaṇe 'ntarvedi brahmabhāgaṃ sādayaty aparaṃ bahirvedi yajamānabhāgam
anvāhāryam anu havīṃṣy udvāsayati
anuyājasamidham ādāyāha brahman prasthāsyāmaḥ samidham ādhāyāgnīt paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca sakṛt sakṛt saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati
idhmasaṃnahanaiḥ saṃmārṣṭi ājiṃ tvāgne sasṛvāṃsaṃ saniṃ sasanivāṃsaṃ vājaṃ jigivāṃsaṃ devebhyo havyam ūhivāṃsaṃ vājinaṃ tvā vājajitaṃ saṃmārjmy agne vājam ajaiṣīr iti
visrasyābhyukṣya saṃmārgān agnāv anupraharati
yo bhūtānām adhipatī rudras tanticaro vṛṣā
paśūn asmākaṃ mā hiṃsīr etad astu hutaṃ tava svāhā
iti
aupabhṛtaṃ juhvām ānīya trīn anuyājān yajati devān yajeti prathame yaja yajety uttarau
samidhy aparam aparam iṣṭvottamenetarāv anusaṃbhidyāyatane srucau sādayati
vājasya meti juhūṃ sahaprastarām udgṛhṇāti
athā sapatnān indro ma ity upabhṛtam avagṛhṇāti
udgrābhaś ceti juhūm
nigrābhaś cety upabhṛtam
athā sapatnān indrāgnī ma iti viṣūcī karoti
agner ujjitim anūjjeṣam iti prācīṃ juhūṃ prakarṣati
devas taṃ savitā pratinudatu yo asmān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma ity upabhṛtaṃ pratīcīṃ bahirvedi nirasyati
abhyukṣya pratyāsādayati
juhvā paridhīn anakti vasur asīti madhyamam upāvasur iti dakṣiṇaṃ viśvāvasur ity uttaram
saṃjānāthāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī iti barhiṣi vidhṛtī visṛjya prastaram anakti pṛthivyām aṅkṣveti dhruvāyāṃ mūlam antarikṣe 'ṅkṣvety upabhṛti madhyaṃ divyaṅkṣveti juhvām agram
pratyavarohaiḥ punar aktvāyuṣe tveti prastarāt tṛṇam apādāya mūlaiḥ pratiṣṭhāpya prastaram āsīna āśrāvya pratyāśruta āha iṣitā daivyā hotāro bhadravācyāya preṣito mānuṣaḥ sūktavākāya sūktā brūhīti saṃpreṣyati
asyām ṛdheddhotrāyām ity ucyamāne sahaśākhaṃ prastaram agnāv anupraharati
aptubhī rihāṇā iti niyataṃ prāñcam anuprahṛtyaināny avasṛjati
agnīd gamayeti saṃpreṣyati
āgnīdhras triḥ pāṇinā gamayati
anuprahara saṃvadasvety āgnīdhraḥ saṃpreṣyati
ahīnaḥ prāṇa ity upāṃśu tṛṇam anupraharati
etad iti trir aṅgulyānudiśati
āyurdhā agne 'sīti yathārūpaṃ gātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
dhruvāsīti pṛthivīm abhimṛśyārcir ālabhya cakṣuṣī ālabheta
punar yamaś cakṣur adāt punar agniḥ punar bhagaḥ
punar me aśvinā yuvaṃ cakṣur ādhattam akṣyoḥ
iti
apaḥ spṛṣṭvā madhyamaṃ paridhim anvārabhyāha agā3n agnīd iti
agann ity āgnīdhraḥ
śrāvayety adhvaryuḥ

svagā daivyāhotṛbhyaḥ svastir mānuṣebhyaḥ śaṃ yor brūhīti saṃpreṣyati

iti paridhīn anupraharati
upakarṣaty uttarārdhyam

agner vo 'pannagṛhasya sadasi sādayāmīti havirdhānaṃ ca kastambhadeśe srucau sādayati

yas taṃ śvo 'gnim ādhāsyan prajā agna iti niśāyāṃ kalmāṣam ajaṃ badhnāti
araṇipāṇir yajamāno jāgarti
śalkair agnim indhāna ubhau lokau sanomy aham
ubhayor lokayor ṛdhnomi mṛtyuṃ tarāmy aham
iti śalkair agnim indhīta
upavyuṣam araṇī niṣṭapati
ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya ity araṇyor agniṃ samāropayati
jātavedo bhuvanasya reta iha siñca tapaso yaj janiṣyate
agnim aśvatthād adhi havyavāhaṃ śamīgarbhāj janayanyo mayobhūḥ
iti ca
ṛtviyavatī stho agniretasau reto dhattaṃ puṣṭyai prajananam
tat satyaṃ yad vīraṃ bibhṛto vīraṃ janayiṣyatas te mat prātaḥ prajanayiṣyete
te mā prajāte prajanayiṣyataḥ prajayā paśubhir brahmavarcasenety araṇī abhimantrya yajamānāya prayacchati
mahī viśpatnī sadanī ṛtasyārvācī etaṃ dharuṇe rayīṇām

anugamayanty agnim uddharanti bhasma
brāhmaudanikalakṣaṇe gārhapatyam ādadhāti purastād āhavanīyam aṣṭasu prakrameṣu brāhmaṇasyaikādaśasu rājanyasya dvādaśasu vaiśyasyāparimite vā
vitṛtīyamātre dakṣiṇāgniṃ dakṣiṇataḥ purastād gārhapatyasya

yat paryapaśyat salilasya madhya urvyā sthānaṃ jagataḥ pratiṣṭhām

iti puṣkaraparṇaṃ nidhāya iyaty agra āsīd ato devī prathamānā pṛthag yad iti varāhavihatam
valmīkavapāṃ nyupyoṣān nivapsyan dhyāyati yad adaś candramasi kṛṣṇaṃ tad ihāstv iti
yad ado divo yad idaṃ pṛthivyāḥ samānaṃ yonim abhisaṃbabhūvathuḥ
tasya pṛṣṭhe sīdatu jātavedāḥ śivaḥ prajābhya iha rāye astu
iti nivapati
candram agniṃ candrarathaṃ harivrataṃ vaiśvānaram apsuṣadaṃ svarvidam
vigāhaṃ tūrṇiṃ taviṣībhir āvṛtaṃ bhūrṇiṃ devāsa iha suśriyaṃ dadhuḥ
iti pravāhā sikatāḥ
śarkarā nivapsyan dveṣyaṃ manasā dhyāyet
adṛṃhathāḥ śarkarābhis triviṣṭapy ajayo lokān pradiśaś catasraḥ
iti nivapati
udehy agne adhi mātuḥ pṛthivyā śiva āviśa mahataḥ sadhasthāt
āśuṃ tvājau dadhire devayanto havyavāhaṃ bhuvanasya gopām
ity ākhukiriṃ nyupya pipīlikākiriṃ goṣṭhāt karīṣāṇi lohaśakalāny aśvattham udumbaraṃ vikaṅkataṃ śamīm aśanihataṃ vṛkṣaṃ palāśam iti nyupya saṃsṛjati
saṃ vaḥ sṛjāmi hṛdayāni vaḥ
ātmā vo astu saṃpriyaḥ saṃpriyās tanvo mama

bhṛgūṇāṃ tveti bhārgavo bhṛgvaṅgirasāṃ tveti bhārgavāṅgirasa ādityānāṃ tvā devānām ity anye
agneṣ ṭvā devasyeti ca
indrasya tveti rājanyo manoṣ ṭveti vaiśya ṛbhūṇāṃ tveti rathakāra āchadi tveti sarveṣām

jvalantam ādhāyeṣe rāye ramasvety abhimantrya sārasvatau tvotsau prāvatām ityantenāgnā āyūṃṣi pavasa iti tisṛbhis tisra āśvatthīḥ samidha ādadhāti

samayādhvaṃ gate tvāhavanīye mathyam āhāryaṃ vā

bhuva iti vyāhṛtiḥ
yatharṣy adhvaryur ādadhāti
gārhapatye 'gnipraṇayanāny ādhāya rathyam aśvaṃ purastāt pratyañcam avasthāpya tasya dakṣiṇakarṇe japati yā vājinn agner iti
ojase balāya tvety agnim udyacchati
śūrpe pāṃsūn nyupyādhastād upayamanīr upayacchati
prācīm anu pradiśam iti praṇayati

na karṇadaghnam aty udyacchati

samayādhve varaṃ dadāti
praṇīyamāne dakṣiṇato brahmā dhūrgṛhītaṃ rathaṃ vartayati
yaḥ sapatnavān bhrātṛvyavān vā syāt tasya rathacakreṇa vihāraṃ trir anuparivartayeyuḥ
abhyasthāṃ viśvā iti purastāt pratyañcam aśvam āhavanīyalakṣaṇam ākrāmayati

antaś caratīti sārparājñī

bhūr bhuvaḥ svariti vyāhṛtir yatharṣyagne havyāya voḍhava ityantena
purastāt pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhan pārśvataḥ padasyādhāyeṣe rāye ramasvety abhimantrya sārasvatau tvotsau prāvatām ityantenāśvenopaghrāpayet
araṇyor nihito jātavedā ity etasyāṃ sāma gāyeti brūyād araṇyor nihitayoḥ
agniṃ naro dīdhitibhir ity etasyāṃ sāma gāyeti brūyāt samavahitayoḥ
tveṣas te dhūma ṛṇvatīty etasyāṃ sāma gāyeti brūyād dhūme
adarśi gātuvittama ity etasyāṃ sāma gāyeti brūyāj jāte
rathantaraṃ gāyati gārhapatya ādhīyamāne

vāmadevyam ādhīyamāne
yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca
nihite vāravantīyaṃ varaṇapāṇir nihite śyaitam

sabhyāt pūrvam āvasathyam
agner manva ity ajaṃ vimucya vācaṃ visṛjya dakṣiṇā dadāti
aśvaṃ vahinaṃ brahmaṇe 'dhvaryave vā
ajam agnīdha upabarhaṇaṃ ca sarvasūtram
kṣaumam idam adhvaryave
purastād vihārasyānaḍvāhaṃ dhenuṃ ca paścāt parītya hotre
dvihāyanamithunau ratha iti sarveṣām avinirdiṣṭam
ṣaḍdvādaśacaturviṃśatyaparimitagavāṃ saṃkhyāvikalpaḥ
anṛtavadanaṃ brāhmaṇopavāsanaṃ svakṛta iriṇe 'vasānam antar nāvy udakācamanam ṛbīsapakvāśanaṃ klinnakāṣṭhābhyādhānam iti varjayet
agnīn upatiṣṭhate yajamānaḥ
paśūn me śaṃsya pāhīty āhavanīyaṃ prajāṃ me narya pāhīti gārhapatyam annaṃ me budhya pāhīti dakṣiṇāgniṃ saprathaḥ sabhāṃ me pāhīti sabhyam ahirbudhnya mantraṃ me pāhīty āvasathyam
āhavanīye nānāvṛkṣīyāḥ samidha ādadhāti tāṃ savitur vareṇyasyeti śamīmayīṃ vidhema ta iti vaikaṅkatīṃ preddho agna ity audumbarīm
yā te agne pavamānā paśuṣu priyā tanūr yā pṛthivyāṃ yāgnau yā rathantare yā gāyatre chandasīdaṃ te tām avarunddhe tasyai te svāhā
yā te agne pāvakāpsu priyā tanūr yāntarikṣe yā vāte yā vāmadevye yā traiṣṭubhe chandasīdaṃ te tām avarunddhe tasyai te svāhā
yā te agne sūrye śuciḥ priyā tanūr yā divi yā bṛhati yā stanayitnau yā jāgate chandasīdaṃ te tām avarunddhe tasyai te svāheti tisra āhutīḥ
samudrād ūrmir iti tisṛbhis tisraḥ śamīmayīr ghṛtāktāḥ samidha ādadhāti
ye agnayaḥ samanasa ity audumbarīm anaktām
kṣuc ca sediś ca snihitiś ca sadānvā cānāmatiś cānāhutiś ca nirṛtir etās te agne tanvo vartimatīs tās taṃ gacchantu yaṃ dviṣma iti dveṣyaṃ manasā dhyāyan yajamāno japati

hutāyāṃ dhenuṃ dadāti
ye agnayo diva iti dvitīyām

gām asya tad ahaḥ sabhāyāṃ vidīvyeyuḥ

tat kṛtaṃ vicinuyāt
ahiṃsantaḥ parūṃṣi viśaṃsyuḥ

uto no 'hirbudhnya iti sabhāvasathyayor juhoti

dhruvam asīti prathamena kapālamantreṇa carum upadadhāti

utsādanīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapaty agnaye vaiśvānarāya dvādaśakapālam

punas tvādityā ity āhavanīyam

agne śundhasvety āhavanīyaṃ parisamūhaty agne gṛhapate śundhasveti gārhapatyam agne vahne śundhasveti dakṣiṇāgnim

saṃtatām udakadhārāṃ srāvayati gārhapatyād adhy āhavanīyād yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtataye nayāmīti
apoḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam apoḍhāḥ senā abhītvarīr iti gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān apohyādhiśrayati
iḍāyās padaṃ ghṛtavac carācaram agne havir idaṃ juṣasva
ye grāmyāḥ paśavo ye cāraṇyās teṣāṃ sarveṣām iha puṣṭir astu
iti
udbhavaḥ sthod ahaṃ prajayā paśubhir bhūyāsam iti jyotiṣāvekṣate
haras te mā vinaiṣam iti sruveṇodabinduṃ pratinayati dadhyājyayoḥ
tena dharmeṇa punar avokṣyāntaritaṃ rakṣo 'ntaritā arātaya iti tṛṇena triḥ paryagniṃ kṛtvā vartma kurvann udag udvāsayati gharmo 'si rāyaspoṣavanir ihorjaṃ śrayasveti
pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayaṃ pratyūḍhāḥ senā abhītvarīr ity aṅgārān pratyūhya niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣo niṣṭaptā arātaya iti sruvaṃ niṣṭapya praṇavam uktvonneṣyāmīti yajamānaṃ sāyam āmantrayata unnayāmīti prātaḥ
agnaye ca tvā pṛthivyai connayāmi
vāyave ca tvāntarikṣāya connayāmi
sūryāya ca tvā dive connayāmi
adbhyaś ca tvauṣadhībhyaś connayāmīti catur unnayati
sarvān pūrṇān yathālābhaṃ vā
yaṃ kāmayetānujyeṣṭhaṃ prajayā ṛdhnuyād iti brāhmaṇavyākhyātam
unnīyā homād vācaṃ yacchet
paśūn me yacchety abhihṛtya sādayati
daśahotrābhimṛśya sajūr devaiḥ sāyaṃyāvabhir iti sāyam unnītam abhimṛśati sajūr devaiḥ prātaryāvabhir iti prātaḥ
idaṃ devānām ity unnītam abhimṛśatīdam u naḥ sahety avaśiṣṭam
urv antarikṣaṃ vīhīti samayā gārhapatyaṃ harati
svāhāgnaye vaiśvānarāya svāheti samayādhve niyacchati
vāyave tvety udyacchati
āyur me yaccheti paścād āhavanīyasya darbheṣu sādayati
eṣā te agne samid ity āhavanīye prādeśamātrīṃ pālāśīṃ samidham ādadhāti
dvyaṅgule jvalantīm abhijuhoti bhūr bhuvaḥ svar agnihotraṃ hotrāgnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyaṃ sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
iṣe tvety avācīnaṃ sāyaṃ lepam avamārṣṭy ūrje tvety ūrdhvaṃ prātaḥ
varco me yaccheti sādayati
oṣadhībhyas tveti darbheṣu lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
prajāpate paśūn me pāhīti gārhapatyam avekṣate
pūrvām asaṃsaktāṃ bhūyasīṃ dvitīyām āhutiṃ juhoti prajāpataye svāheti manasā
anābho mṛḍa dhūrta iti trir udīcīṃ srucam uddharati
tena dharmeṇonmṛjyāvamṛjya vā prajāṃ me yaccheti sādayati
pitṝñ jinveti dakṣiṇataḥ pṛthivyāṃ lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
apaḥ spṛṣṭvā pūṣāsīti dvir aṅgulyā prāśnāti
na dato gamayet
udagdaṇḍayā srucāntarvedi bhakṣayati garbhān prīṇāti garbhebhyaḥ svāheti
nirasya lepaṃ paristaraṇaiḥ srucaṃ prakṣālyotkaraṃ pradāya pūrayitvā prāgudīcīm utsiñcati sarpān pipīlikāḥ prīṇāti sarpebhyaḥ pipīlikābhyaś ca svāheti
dvitīyaṃ paścād āhavanīyasya pṛthivyām amṛtaṃ juhomi svāheti
srucaṃ niṣṭapya hastam avadhāyottarato nidadhāti saptaṛṣīn prīṇāti saptaṛṣibhyaḥ svāheti
yathākāmy aparayor homo 'gne gṛhapate pariṣadya juṣasva svāhety ekasruvaṃ vigṛhṇāti dakṣiṇāgnau cāgnaye puṣṭipataye svāheti prājāpatya uttare
antarvedi prakṣālanaṃ ninayati sarpadevajanān prīṇāti sarpadevajanebhyaḥ svāheti
dīdihi dīdāya dīdidāya svāheti paryāyaiḥ sarveṣu samidha ādhāya tena dharmeṇa paryukṣati
payasā juhuyāt paśukāmasya yavāgvā grāmakāmasyājyena tejaskāmasya dadhnendriyakāmasya taṇḍulair balakāmasya
dvādaśarātram ājyena dadhnā dvādaśarātram
nityaṃ payo yavāguś ca
payo'bhāve yavāgur aśuṣkā
dvayor gavoḥ sthālyā dohanena ca dohayitvā paśukāmasya juhuyāt
sajūr jātavedo divā pṛthivyā juṣāṇo asya haviṣo vīhi svāheti juhuyād yatra rudraḥ paśūn abhimanyeta
ājyam agnihotram
yadi nāramed agne duḥśīrtatano juṣasva svāheti juhuyāt
yadi nāramed dvādaśarātraṃ sāyaṃ sāyaṃ juhuyāt
anarhato rājanyasya parvasv agnihotraṃ juhuyān nāntarāle
sāyaṃ prātar agraṃ bhaktasya brāhmaṇakulaṃ hared agnyupasthānaṃ ca vācayet
saṃtatam arhato juhuyāt
sāyaṃ patny anvāste na prātaḥ
hiṃkṛtya striyam upeyāt
sūryoḍham atithiṃ nāparundhīta
na sāyam ahute 'gnihotre 'śnīyān na prātaḥ
vasantā śiśire kakṣaṃ dahet
adhiśrite 'gnihotre mamāgne varca iti catasṛbhir vaihavībhir hastāv avanenijīta purastād agnīṣomīyāyā uttarāś catasro japet
vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ity apa upaspṛśya tiṣṭhet
unnīyamāne vācaṃ yacchati
abhyudāhṛta upaviśya daśahotrābhimṛśyottarām āhutim upotthāyopaprayanto adhvaram iti prāgudaṅmukhaś caturbhir anuvākair āhavanīyam upatiṣṭheta
agnīṣomīyayā pūrvapakṣa aindrāgnyāparapakṣe
agnā āyūṃṣi pavasa iti ṣaḍbhir āhavanīyaṃ nityaṃ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare gārhapatyam
agneḥ samid asīti paryāyair āhavanīye samidha ādadhāti
citrāvaso svasti te pāram aśīyārvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīyeti trir japati
prātarupasthāne cāmbhaḥ sthāmbho vo bhakṣīyeti gṛhān upatiṣṭhate
revatī ramadhvam ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhan japati
saṃhitāsi viśvarūpeti vaśām ālabhate vatsaṃ vā
upa tvāgne dive diva iti gārhapatyam
abhyasthāṃ viśvā ity āhavanīyam
ūrjā vaḥ paśyāmy ūrjā mā paśyateti gṛhān paśūn abhivīkṣate
iḍāḥ stheti gām ālabhate bhuvanam asīti vatsam
nimrado 'sīti brāhmaṇavyākhyātam
prācī dig iti paryāyair diśa upatiṣṭhate
agne gṛhapata iti gārhapatyaṃ yathā yājamāne
jyotiṣe tantave tvety antarvedy upaviśyāhavanīye 'bhyādhāya vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpmānam ity apa upaspṛśet
prātaravanegena prātar upatiṣṭheta
apāṃ pate yo 'pāṃ bhāgaḥ sa ta eṣa iti prāgudañcam udakāñjalim utsicya pratiṣiktā arātaya iti triḥ pratyukṣati
kālāya vām iti pāṇī prakṣālyedam ahaṃ duradmanyāṃ niṣplāvayāmīty ācamya niṣṭhīvati
bhrātṛvyāṇāṃ sapatnānām iti pāṇī prakṣālayate
indriyavatīm adyeti yathārūpaṃ gātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
ado mā mā hāsiṣṭeti pāṇī prakṣālayate
sūryapatnīr ity abhiṣiñcan purudhyavāno mahiṣa iti ca hute catasro vaihavīr uktvā gharmo jaṭhare ity anuvākenāhavanīyam upatiṣṭheta
asau svasti te 'stvasau svasti te 'stviti nāmagrāhaṃ putrān anvātayate
agnīn samādhehīty āha pravatsyan
bhāsvata upatiṣṭhate
paśūn me śaṃsya pāhīty āhavanīyaṃ prajāṃ me narya pāhīti gārhapatyam annaṃ me budhya pāhīti dakṣiṇāgniṃ saprathaḥ sabhāṃ me pāhīti sabhyam ahirbudhnya mantraṃ me pāhīty āvasathyam
imān me mitrāvaruṇau gṛhān gopāyataṃ yuvam ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhan japati
mama nāma prathamaṃ jātavedaḥ pitā mātā ca dadhatur nv agre
tat tvaṃ bibhṛhi punar ā mamaitos tanvāham agne bibharāṇi nāma
ity āhavanīyam
mā pragāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ
māntaḥ sthur no arātayaḥ
yo yajñasya prasādhanas tantur deveṣv ātataḥ
tam āhutaṃ naśīmahi
iti vrajati
sakāśe vācaṃ yacchaty asakāśe visṛjate
yathākālam agnyupasthānayājamāne japet
proṣya samidha āharati
asakāśe vācaṃ yacchati sakāśe visṛjate
agnīn samādhehīty āha
proṣya bhāsvata upatiṣṭhate
agneḥ samid asīti paryāyaiḥ sarveṣu samidha ādhāya viśvadānīm ābharanto 'nātureṇa manasā
agne mā te prativeśā riṣāma
ity āhavanīyaṃ paśūn me śaṃsyājugupa iti ca
prajāṃ me naryājugupa iti gārhapatyam annaṃ me budhyājugupa iti dakṣiṇāgniṃ saprathaḥ sabhāṃ me 'jugupas tāṃ me punar dehīti sabhyam ahirbudhnya mantraṃ me 'jugupas taṃ me punar dehīty āvasathyam
imān me mitrāvaruṇau gṛhān ajugupataṃ yuvam ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhan japati
mama ca nāma tava ca jātavedo vāsasī iva vivasānau carāvaḥ
te bibhṛto mahase jīvase ca yathāyathaṃ nau tanvau jātavedaḥ
ity āhavanīyam
nava rātrīḥ parārdhāḥ proṣyāhutiṃ juhoti viśvakarman haviṣā ghṛtena vicchinnaṃ yajñaṃ samimaṃ dadhātu
yā iṣṭā uṣaso yāśca yājyās tāḥ saṃdadhāmi manasā ghṛtena
iti
nava rātrīḥ parārdhā uṣitvā sahagṛhaḥ prayāsyan yukteṣu cakrāvatsu vāstoṣpatyaṃ juhoti
na hīnam anvāhareyuḥ
amīvahā vāstoṣpate
vāstoṣpata ity etābhyām āhutī hutvāyaṃ te yonir ṛtviya ity araṇyor agniṃ samāropayati gārhapatyāhavanīyau gataśriyo gārhapatyam agataśriyaḥ
dakṣiṇāgnir yadi mathyaḥ samāropayet
yady araṇyor nāśam āśaṅketa sakṣehi yā te yajñiyā tanūs tayehy ārohety ātmani vihāraṃ samāropayati
na sahāgnir ṛte gṛhebhyaḥ pravaset
nāsaṃdahyāvakṣāṇāni prayāyāt
upāvaroha jātavedo devebhyo havyaṃ vahatu prajānan
āyuḥ prajāṃ rayim asmāsu dhehy ariṣṭo dīdihi no duroṇe
ity upāvarohya manthet
śyāmākān bubhukṣamāṇaḥ purāṇānāṃ vrīhīṇām āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet saumyaṃ ca śyāmākaṃ carum
babhruḥ piśaṅgo dakṣiṇā vasanaṃ vā
vrīhīṇām agrapākasya yajate yavānāṃ ca
nāniṣṭvāgrāyaṇena navasyāśnīta
aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvaped āgnendraṃ vā
vaiśvadevaḥ payasi caruḥ śyāmākaś caruḥ
na yavāgrāyaṇe
dyāvāpṛthivīya ekakapāla iti havīṃṣi
purastāt sviṣṭakṛto 'jyānīr juhoti
śatāyudhāya śatavīryāya śatotaye 'bhimātiṣāhe
śataṃ yo naḥ śarado 'nayad indro duritasya pāraṃ svāhā
ye catvāraḥ pathayo devayānā antarā dyāvāpṛthivī viyanti
teṣām ajyānīṃ yatamo na āvahat tasmai no devāḥ paridatta sarve svāhā
vasanto grīṣmo madhumanti varṣāḥ śaraddhemantaḥ suvite dadhāta naḥ
teṣāṃ vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyānāṃ jyog ajītā ahatāḥ syāma svāhā
svasti saṃvatsarāya parivatsarāyedāvatsarāyodvatsarāya kṛṇutā bṛhan namaḥ
teṣāṃ vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyānāṃ nivāta eṣām abhaye syāma svāhā
iyaṃ svasti saṃvatsarīyā parivatsarīyedāvatsarīyodvatsarīyā
sā naḥ pipartv ahṛṇīyamānenāhedahāram aśīya svāhā
iti
ā naḥ prajāṃ janayatv iti ṣaṣṭhī
iḍāṃ bhakṣayati
bhadrān naḥ śreyaḥ samanaiṣṭa devās tvayāvasena samaśīmahi tvā
sa no mayobhūḥ pitur āviveśa śivas tokāya tanvo na edhi
iti vrīhīṇām
agniḥ prāśnātu prathamaḥ sa hi veda yathā haviḥ
śivā asmabhyam oṣadhīḥ kṛṇotu viśvacarṣaṇiḥ
iti śyāmākānām
etam u tyaṃ madhunā saṃyutaṃ yavaṃ sarasvatyā adhi manāv acakṛṣuḥ
indra āsīt sīrapatiḥ śatakratuḥ kīnāśā āsan marutaḥ sudānavaḥ
iti yavānām
vatsaḥ prathamajo dakṣiṇā vatsaḥ prathamajo dakṣiṇā
udagayanasyādyantayor aindrāgnena paśunā yajeta saṃvatsare saṃvatsare vā
ṣaḍḍhotrā manasā juhoti vāgghotā dīkṣā patny āpo 'dhvaryur vāto 'bhigaraḥ prāṇo havir mano brahmā tapasi juhomi svāheti
graheṇa dvitīyām vācaspate 'chidrayā vācāchidrayā juhvā divi devāmṛdaṃ hotrām airayaṃ svāheti
āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvapati vaiṣṇavīṃ vā pūrṇāhutim
uru viṣṇo vikramasveti vaiṣṇavyā hutvā yūpam acchaiti bilvapalāśakhadirarohitakodumbarāṇām ekam
bailvaṃ brahmavarcasakāmaḥ kurvīta
pañcāratnyādipramāṇam anadhiśākhyam ṛjum ūrdhvaśalkam upariṣṭād upāvanataṃ bahupalāśaśākham apratiśuṣkāgraṃ prāñcaṃ pratyañcaṃ vāhānam
aty anyān agām ity abhimantrya viṣṇave tvety ājyena paryanakti
oṣadhe trāyasvainam iti darbham antardadhāti
svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti paraśunā praharati
prathamaśalkam upayamya bhūmisamaṃ vṛścati
yaṃ tvām ayaṃ svadhitir iti prāñcaṃ prahāpayati
vanaspate śatavalśo virohety āvraścane juhoti
sahasravalśā ity ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati
aṣṭāśriṃ takṣati gopuccham ataṣṭamūlam
agrato 'gniṣṭhāṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ sūryasthām
agrasya caṣālaṃ pṛthamātram aṣṭāśri madhye saṃgṛhītam
idhmābarhiḥ saṃnahya vedaṃ kṛtvā rathamātrīṃ vediṃ karoti śamyāmātrīm uttaravedim
yat prāg uttarasmāt parigrāhāt tat kṛtvā sāvitreṇābhrim ādāyābhrir asi nārir asīty abhimantryottarata uttaravedyantāt prakramamātre cātvālaṃ parilikhati taptāyanī me 'sīti paryāyair dikṣu śamyāṃ nidhāyānuśamyamabhrathā vyavalikhati
jānudaghnaṃ caturaśraṃ khātvottaravedyai pāṃsūn harati
vider agna iti khanati
agne aṅgira ity avadāya vasavas tvā harantv iti harati
vitsva yajñapater iti paścād yūpāvaṭasya nivapati
etena dharmeṇottarābhyāṃ paryāyābhyāṃ trir yajuṣā harati tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
samānaḥ khanano nivapanaś ca
devebhyaḥ prathasvety uttaravediṃ prathayati
devebhyaḥ kalpayasveti kalpayati
caturaśrām uttaravedyāṃ prādeśamātrīṃ nābhiṃ kṛtvā siṃhīr asi mahiṣīr asīty abhimantrya devebhyaḥ śundhasvety uttaravediṃ prokṣati
devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti sikatābhiḥ prarocayati
adbhir niḥsārayati saṃtatām udakadhārāṃ srāvayan sphyena vartma kṛtvā samayottarāv asāv āpo ripraṃ nirvahateti
prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtyottaravediṃ prokṣati indra ghoṣās tveti paryāyair anuparikrāman
pitṝṇāṃ bhāgadheyīḥ stheti dakṣiṇata uttaravedyāḥ prokṣaṇīśeṣaṃ ninīya pañcagṛhītenājyenottaravediṃ vyāghārayati hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya siṃhīr asi sapatnasāhī svāheti paryāyair akṣṇayā śroṇyaṃseṣu
madhye pañcamena
bhūtebhyas tveti trir udīcīṃ srucam uddiśati
nābhyāṃ pautudravān paridhīn paridadhāti prādeśamātrān viśvāyur asīti paryāyaiḥ
aver anācchinnastukasyāntarā śṛṅgād ūrṇāstukāṃ kerugulgulv iti nābhyāṃ saṃbhārān nivapati
agner bhasmāsīti paryāyair vibhrāḍ bṛhad ity āntād anuvākasyottaravedim abhimṛśyāhavanīyād agniṃ praṇayati
yat te pāvaka cakṛmā kaccid āgaḥ pūrvo yaḥ sann aparo bhavati
ghṛtenāgne tanvaṃ vardhayasva mā mā hiṃsīr adhigataṃ purastāt
ity udyate 'gnāv āhavanīye juhoti
agnaye praṇīyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
upayacchaty upayamanīḥ
ūrṇāvantam ity ucyamāne
yajñaḥ pratyaṣṭhāt sumatiḥ sumedhā ā tvā vasūni purodhārhanti
dīrgham āyur yajamānāya kṛṇvann athāmṛtena jaritāram aṅdhi
iti saṃbhāreṣv adhvaryur agniṃ sādayati
yasmād adhi praṇayati tasmin gārhapatyakarmāṇi kurvītāgnihotraṃ ca juhuyād auttaravedike
varuṇapraghāseṣv agnihotraṃ praṇayanī pūrṇāhutir iti yathāgnyādheye
atimuktīr juhoti
agnir yajñaṃ nayatu prajānan mainaṃ yajñahano vidan
devebhyo yajñaṃ nayatāt pra pra yajñapatiṃ tira svāhā
iti
vāyuḥ sūryo yajñaṃ nayatv iti samānam
praṇīte 'gnyanvādhānaṃ vratopāyanam
pāṇiprakṣālanaprabhṛti samānam ā pātraprayogāt
ekādaśakapālaḥ puroḍāśo dvādaśakapālo vā
dve juhve vasāhomahavanī dvitīyā
dve upabhṛtau pṛṣadājyadhānī dvitīyā
dve ājyasthālyau
yūpaśalkam
śūlam
paśūkhām
kārṣmaryamayyau vapāśrapaṇyau
dviśṛṅgaikaśṛṅge
audumbaram āsyadaghnaṃ maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍam
darbhāṇāṃ raśane dviguṇāṃ dvivyāyāmāṃ triguṇāṃ trivyāyāmāṃ saṃsādya prokṣya pātrāṇy ājyaṃ nirvapati dadhi ca
pṛṣadājyadhūmair dadhi saṃskaroty upabhṛddharmaiḥ pṛṣadājyadhānīṃ pātrāṇi ca pātradharmaiḥ dvitīyāni
sphyaprakṣālanaprabhṛti samānam ājyagrahebhyaḥ
catur upabhṛti gṛhītvā pañcagṛhītaṃ pṛṣadājyadhānyām ājyena saṃnīya mahīnāṃ payo 'si viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ tanūrasi
ṛdhyāsam adya pṛṣatīnāṃ graham
pṛṣatīnāṃ graho 'si viṣṇor hṛdayam asīti paryāyaiḥ
sanneṣv ājyeṣu yūpāvaṭaṃ parilikhati idam ahaṃ rakṣaso grīvā apikṛntāmīti pūrvasya vedyantasya madhye 'rdham antarvedy ardhaṃ bahirvedi
uttarataś cātvālasya śāmitralakṣaṇam uddhanti
yat te śociḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā
āpas tat pāvakāḥ śundhantu śucayaḥ śucim
iti snātaṃ yūpaṃ tīrthenopasādya tūṣṇīkāṃ yavamatīḥ prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya yūpaṃ prokṣati pṛthivyai tveti mūlam antarikṣāya tveti madhyaṃ dive tvety agram
śundhantāṃ lokā iti yūpāvaṭam
yavo 'sīti yavān avadadhāti
pitṛṣadanaṃ tveti darbhair avastṛṇāti
svāveśo 'sīti prathamaśalkam avadhāya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī iti sruveṇābhijuhoti
purastāt pratyañcaṃ yajamāno yūpam anakti
yūpāyājyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
āntam avicchinnam anakti
devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti yūpāgram anakti
sarvaṃ sahacaṣālam anakti indrasya caṣālam asīti
caṣālaṃ pratimucya supippalā oṣadhīr ity aṅgulimātram ūrdhvaṃ caṣālād yūpāgraṃ kanīyo vā
yūpāyocchrīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
divam agreṇottabhānety ucchrayati
tā te dhāmānīty avadadhāti
viṣṇoḥ karmāṇīty avasthāpayaty agnim abhimukhīm agniṣṭhām
na taṣṭasya nikhanati
nātaṣṭasyāviṣkaroti
brahmavaniṃ tveti pāṃsubhiḥ parivapati
brahma dṛṃha kṣatraṃ dṛṃheti yajamāno maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍena paridṛṃhayati
prokṣaṇīśeṣeṇa pariṣicya tad viṣṇor iti svaruraśanena samunmārṣṭi
divīva cakṣur ātatam iti saṃmitam abhimantrayate
trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivyayaty agrato raśanāyās triḥ pariharaṇāya yūpāyāvaśiṣya śeṣaṃ dvaidhaṃ saṃbhujyottarataḥ sūryasthāyā nābhimātre saṃbhogaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yūpāya parivīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
parivīr asīti triḥ parivyayaty uttaram uttaraṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ saṃbhoge raśanāgram atihṛtya mūlato nirāyamyāntāt praveṣṭayati
śraṇīyasīṃ sthavīyasy upakarṣati
yadi kāmayeta varṣety parjanya iti
añjanādi yajamāno yūpaṃ nāparivītam avasṛjati
divaḥ sānūpeṣety uttame raśanāguṇe svarum upakṛṣyājam upākaroti śvetaṃ lohitaṃ dvirūpaṃ vā śmaśrulam
kūṭākarṇakāṇakhaṇḍabaṇḍāpannadanta iti pratiṣiddhāḥ
uttarato yūpasya pratyañcaṃ paśum avasthāpyāhutī juhoti
prajāpater jāyamānāḥ prajā jātāś ca yā imāḥ
tā asmai prativedaya cikitvam anumanyatām
imaṃ paśuṃ paśupate te 'dya badhnāmy agne salilasya madhye
anumanyasva suyajā yajeha juṣṭaṃ devebhya idam astu havyam
iti
iṣe tveti darbhāv ādatte
upāvīr asīti plakṣaśākhāṃ hariṇīṃ palāśavatīm
tayā darbhābhyāṃ ca paśum upākaroti upo devān iti
pratyañcaṃ paśum anumārṣṭi amuṣmai tvā juṣṭam iti yathādevatam
abhidhānaprokṣaṇavapotkhedanābhighāraṇeṣu
paścān madhyamasya paridher adhimanthanaṃ śakalaṃ prayunakti agner janitram asīti vṛṣaṇau stha ity apracchinnaprāntau darbhau
tayor adhy urvaśyasīty udakkūlāṃ pratyakprajananām adharāraṇim
āyur asīty ājyasthālyām uttarāraṇim anakti sampādayati ca
purūravā asīty abhimantrya gāyatram asīti paryāyais trir abhimathyāgnaye mathyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
agnaye jātāyeti jāte
agnaye prahriyamāṇāyeti prahariṣyan
agreṇottaraṃ paridhim uttareṇa vā paridhisaṃdhinānvavahṛtya bhavataṃ naḥ samanasāv ity anuprahṛtyāgnā agnir iti sruveṇābhijuhoti
sāvitreṇa raśanām ādāya bāhuṃ paśor medhyapāśena parihṛtya dakṣiṇārdhaśiro 'kṣṇayā pāśenābhidadhāti ṛtasya tvā devahavir iti
dharṣā mānuṣā iti yūpe niyunakti
prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya paśuṃ prokṣati adbhyas tvauṣadhībhya iti
anu tvā mātā manyatām ity abhimantryāpāṃ perur asīti pāyayati
svāttaṃ saddhavir iti śeṣeṇa sarvata upokṣya saṃmṛśyājyāni vedyantān paristīrya hotṛṣadanān āstīryāgnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
sraucam āghārya dhruvāṃ samajya paśuṃ samanakti saṃ te vāyur iti prāṇadeśaṃ saṃ yajatrair aṅgānīti kakubdeśaṃ saṃ yajñapatir āśiṣeti bhasaddeśam
prayājeṣu samidbhyaḥ preṣyeti prathamaṃ saṃpreṣyati preṣya preṣyety uttarān
caturthe caturthe samānayati
daśabhiḥ pracarya svaruṃ svadhitidhārāṃ ca juhvām aktvā svaruṇā svadhitim antardhāya paśor antarāśṛṅgam anakti ghṛtenāktau paśūṃs trāyethām iti
āyatane srucau sādayati
āhavanīyād ulmukam upayamya paryagnaye kriyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
śāmitraṃ cātvālaṃ paśum āhavanīyaṃ yūpam ājyānīty āgnīdhras triḥ paryagnikṛtvāhavanīya ulmukam avasṛjya triḥ pratiparyeti
ye badhyamānam iti paśupramocanīyā juhoti
revatīti vapāśrapaṇībhyāṃ paśum anvārabhate yajamānaś ca
tad evolmukam upayamyāgnīdhro 'grataḥ pratipadyeta
anvārabhyāśrāvayati
ulmukapāṇir āgnīdhraḥ pratyāśrāvayati upapreṣya hotar havyā devebhya iti saṃpreṣyati
uro antarikṣety agnimukhās tīrthenodañco vrajanti
śāmitralakṣaṇe 'gniṃ sādayati
tasmin paśuṃ śrapayati
paścācchāmitrasya yābhyāṃ darbhābhyāṃ paśum upākaroti tayor anyataram adhastād upāsyati sam asya tanvā bhaveti
varṣīyo varṣīyasa iti yajamāno japati
nānā prāṇo yajamānasya paśunā yajño devebhiḥ saha devayānaḥ
samyag āyur yajño yajñapatau dadhātu
iti paryāvṛtyeha prajā viśvarūpā ramantām iti pṛṣadājyam avekṣate yajamānaś ca
pratyakśirasam udīcīnapādaṃ saṃjñapayanti
svarvid asīti yajamānaḥ saṃjñapyamānam anumantrayate
na vā etan mriyasa ity adhvaryuḥ
yat paśur māyum akṛtoro vā paḍbhir āhate
agnir mā tasmād enaso viśvān muñcatv aṃhasaḥ
iti saṃjñapte juhoti
śamitāra upetaneti saṃpreṣyati
paścāt paśum iti pāśeṣu pramucyamāneṣu japati
ekaśṛṅgayā pāśāṃś cātvāle 'nupraharati
yo no dveṣṭy adharaḥ sa padyatām iti yady abhicaret
stambaṃ sthāṇuṃ vāpidadhyāt
śatena pāśair varuṇābhidhehi mā te mocy anṛtavāṅ nṛcakṣaḥ
āstāṃ jālma udaraṃ sraṃsayitvā kośa ivābandhraḥ parikṛtyamānaḥ
iti
namas ta ātāneti patny ādityam upatiṣṭhate
anarvā prehīty enām abhyudānayate
devīr āpa ity adhy adhi cātvālaṃ patny apo 'vamarśayati
tābhyaḥ patnī paśoḥ prāṇān prakṣālayaty adhvaryur vā
anyataro 'bhiṣiñcet
vācamasya mā hiṃsīr iti yathārūpaṃ gātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
yat te krūraṃ yad āsthitam iti pūrvaś cānuṣajet
gātrāṇy asya mā hiṃsīr iti grīvāḥ pṛṣṭhadeśaṃ śam adbhya iti śeṣeṇa sarvataḥ
uttānaṃ paryāvṛtyopākaraṇaṃ darbham antardadhāti
oṣadhe trāyasvainam iti darbham antardadhāti
svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr ity anaktataḥ svadhitinā tiryag āchyati
upayacchati tṛṇāgram
lohitāktaṃ pratyagdakṣiṇā nirasyati pṛthivyai tvā rakṣasāṃ bhāgo 'sīti
idam ahaṃ rakṣo 'vabādha idam ahaṃ rakṣo 'dhamaṃ tamo nayāmīti pārṣṇyā tṛṇam avabādhate
apaḥ spṛṣṭveṣe tveti vapām utkhidati
ūrje tveti taniṣṭha ekaśṛṅgayopatṛṇatti
devebhyaḥ śundhasveti vapāṃ prakṣālayati
devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti lohitaṃ pratyūhati
ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī iti dviśṛṅgāṃ pracchādyotkṛtya namaḥ sūryasya saṃdṛśa ity ādityam upasthāyorv antarikṣaṃ vīhīti vrajati
pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣa iti śāmitre vapāṃ pratyoṣati
tvām u te dadhire devayanto havyavāhaṃ śṛtaṃ kartāram uta yajñiyaṃ ca
agniḥ sudakṣaḥ sutanur ha bhūtvā devebhyo havyā vaha jātavedaḥ
iti sruveṇābhighārya stokebhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
śyenīṃ śṛtāṃ barhiṣy āsādayati supippalā oṣadhīs kṛdhīti
vapāśrapaṇyau vipramucyottamena prayājena pracarati
svāhākṛtibhyaḥ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
hutvā dhruvāṃ pṛṣadājyaṃ vapām ity abhighārayati
yathākāmyājyabhāgayor homaḥ
sarvahutaṃ vapāṃ juhoti
abhito vapāṃ hiraṇyaśakalāv avadyati
svāhā devebhya iti purastād vapāyāḥ sruveṇa juhoti viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ svāhety upariṣṭāt
indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāyā medaso 'nubrūhi
indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāyā medasaḥ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
jātavedo vapayā gaccha devāṃs tvaṃ hi hotā prathamo babhūva
ghṛtenāgne tanvaṃ vardhayasva satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmāḥ
iti vapāṃ hutvā svāhordhvanabhasam iti vyatyaste vapāśrapaṇyāv anupraharati prācīm ekaśṛṅgāṃ pratīcīṃ dviśṛṅgām
saṃpātenābhihutyāyatane srucau sādayati
cātvāla āpohiṣṭhīyena tryṛcena mārjayante sahayajamānapatnīkāḥ
atraiva madhumanthānāṃ kālaḥ
muṣṭinā śamitā vapoddharaṇam abhidhāyāsta ā vapāyā homāt
ukhāyāṃ paśuṃ śrapayati śūle hṛdayam
na gudaṃ nirvleṣayen na vaniṣṭhum
medo mūta upanahyati
ūvadhyagohaṃ khātvovadhyaṃ gūhati
vrīhīṇāṃ paśunā samānadevataṃ paśupuroḍāśaṃ śrapayati
śṛte paśau paśupuroḍāśena pracarati
indrāgnibhyāṃ puroḍāśasyānubrūhi
indrāgnibhyāṃ puroḍāśasya preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
agnaye 'nubrūhīti
agnaye preṣyeti sviṣṭakṛte
iḍāntaṃ kṛtvā pṛṣadājyasya sruveṇopahatya paraiti
śṛtaṃ haviḥ śamitā iti pṛcchati
śṛtam iti śamitā pratyāha
samayādhve dvitīyam
prāpya tṛtīyam
uttarato 'vasthāya hṛdayam avadhāya juṣṭaṃ devebhya ity abhighārya vivājinaṃ kṛtvāntarā yūpāhavanīyāv atihṛtya dakṣiṇataḥ pañcahotropasādayati
juhūpabhṛtor vasāhomahavanyāṃ samavattadhānyām ity upastīrya plakṣaśākhāyāṃ hṛdayam avadhāyāktayāvadyan manotāyai haviṣo 'vadīyamānasyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
hṛdayasya jihvāyāḥ kroḍasya savyasya kapilalāṭasya pārśvayor yakno vṛkkayor dakṣiṇasyāḥ śroṇyāḥ gudatṛtīyam iti dvir dvir avadāya juhvām avadyati
tridhā gudaṃ vicchidyāsyāṇīyaso devatābhyo 'vadyati
sthaviṣṭhagudasyopayaḍbhyo nidadhāti
dakṣiṇasya kapilalāṭasya pūrvārdhān madhyamaṃ gudatṛtīyaṃ savyāyāḥ śroṇyā jaghanārdhāt sakṛt sakṛd upabhṛti sviṣṭakṛte
yūṣe medaḥ pariplāvya traidhaṃ vicchidya juhūpabhṛtau pracchādayati
śeṣam iḍāyām abhito daivatāni hiraṇyaśakalāv avadyati
reḍ asīti svadhitinā vasāhomaṃ prayauti
prayutā dveṣāṃsīti pārśvenāpas tvā samariṇvann iti gṛhītvā pārśvenāpidadhāti
anusuṃ ṣaḍiḍām avadyati vaniṣṭhuṃ saptamam
klomānaṃ purītatam iti saṃkṛtya vardhayitveḍāṃ yūṣeṇopasicya pratiparītya pracarati
indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya haviṣo 'nubrūhi
indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya haviṣaḥ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
ghṛtaṃ ghṛtapāvāna ity ardharce yājyāyā vasāhomaṃ juhoti
pṛṣadājyena sakṛd eva tena vanaspatiṃ yajati
vanaspataye 'nubrūhi
vanaspataye preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
vasām aśeṣeṇa diśaḥ prati yajati
diśaḥ svāheti paryāyaiḥ pratidiśam
madhye pañcamena pūrvārdhe ṣaṣṭhena
aupabhṛtaṃ juhvām avanīya sviṣṭakṛtā pracarati
aindraḥ prāṇa iti yajamānaḥ paśuṃ saṃmṛśaty avadānavantam
upahūtāyām iḍāyām adhyūdhnīṃ hotre haranti
vaniṣṭhum agnīdha ādadhāti yathāgnīdhrabhāgam
dakṣiṇāsan mārjanasaṃpreṣam uktvāgnīd aupayajāṅgārān āharopayaṣṭar upasīdasveti saṃpreṣyati
śāmitrād āgnīdhro 'ṅgārān paścārdhe vedyā vyūhyopasamādadhāti
uttarato dakṣiṇāmukha upaviśya tasmin pratiprasthātopayajati gudakāṇḍam ekādaśadhā sambhindann avadāya vaṣaṭkārānteṣv anuyājānām ekaikaṃ hastena juhoti
samudraṃ gaccha svāheti paryāyair ekādaśa hutvā mano hārdiṃ yaccheti hṛdayadeśam abhimṛśati
oṣadhībhyas tveti darbheṣu nimārṣṭi
apaḥ spṛṣṭvā pṛṣadājyenānuyājān yajati
devebhyaḥ preṣyeti prathame saṃpreṣyati preṣyety uttarān
ekādaśabhiḥ pracarya svaruṃ juhvāṃ trir upariṣṭāt trir adhastād aktvā dadhāti divaṃ te dhūmo gacchatv iti
ūrdhvaṃ svaruhomāt prāg anudeśād yūpo nopaspṛśyaḥ
sūktavāke sūktā preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
jāghanyā patnīḥ saṃyājayaty uttānāyā devānāṃ patnībhyo 'vadyatīḍāṃ cāgnaye gṛhapataye cāgnīdhe ca
yajñaṃ gaccha svāheti paryāyais trīṇi samiṣṭayajūṃṣi juhoti
purastān nityasya tṛtīyaḥ svāhākāraḥ pūrṇapātrasthāne
śūlenāvabhṛthaṃ yanti
parogoṣṭhaṃ yad ārdram anudakam anauṣadhikaṃ ca tasmin śamitopavapati
śug asi yaṃ dviṣmas tam abhiśocety upopyamānam anumantrayate
dhāmno dhāmno rājann ity āntād anuvākasyādhy adhi mārjayitvā samidhaḥ kṛtvānapekṣamāṇāḥ pratyāyanti edho 'sy edhiṣīmahi svāhety āhavanīye samidham ādadhāti
samid asi samedhiṣīmahīti dvitīyām
tat satyaṃ tañ śakeyaṃ tena śakeyaṃ tena rādhyāsam iti yajamāno japati
caturo māsān na māṃsam aśnīyān na striyam upaiti nopary āste jugupsetānṛtāt prāṅ śete
madhv aśnāty ṛtau bhāryām upaiti
sarveṣv antarālavratāni vaiśvadevottarāṇi sahapañcasaṃcarāṇi
parvāṇi vyākhyātāni
vikārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
caturṣu māseṣu varuṇapraghāsāḥ
pratiprasthātāmikṣāyai mārutyai vatsān apākaroty adhvaryur vāruṇyai
pratiprasthātuḥ payasi
pūrvakarmādhvaryor ārāt
pūrvedyur agnipraṇayanam
vedī kuruta uttarām adhvaryur dakṣiṇāṃ pratiprasthātā
asaṃbhinne same
pṛthamātram antarā
uttarasyām uttaravedisaṃbhārān nyupyāhavanīyād agnī praṇayataḥ
agnibhyāṃ praṇīyamānābhyām anubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
agreṇottarāṃ vediṃ pratiprasthātāntarā vedī pratiprasthātā
pātrāṇi prayunakti
avinirdeśe samānam ubhayoḥ karma
yathā vaiśvadeve havīṃṣy oṣadhapātrāṇi
āmantraṇādi prāṇītāḥ saṃpraiṣān mārutīvarjaṃ nirmanthyaṃ pracaratimiḍām ity adhvaryur eva patnīsaṃyājaprabhṛti
samāno hotā brahmāgnīdhraḥ utkaraḥ
pañca saṃcarāṇyaindrāgno dvādaśakapālo māruty āmikṣā vāruṇy āmikṣā kāya ekakapālo vājinam iti havīṃṣi
nirupteṣu pratiprasthātā tūṣṇīko yavān nyupyāmapeṣāṇāṃ karambhapātrāṇi karoti pratipuruṣaṃ yajamānasyaikaṃ cāṅguṣṭhaparvamātrāṇy ekoddhīni
śamīparṇaiḥ pūrayitvā śeṣasya meṣaṃ ca meṣīṃ ca kurutaḥ
niktābhir ūrṇābhir āveṣṭya paraḥśatāni śamīparṇāni ghāsaṃ nivapataḥ
uttaraiḥ parigrāhaiḥ parigṛhya dakṣiṇasyā vedyā uttarasyāḥ śroṇyā adhy uttarasyā ā dakṣiṇād aṃsāt sphyena vedī sambhinatti
pṛṣadājye gṛhṇītaḥ sakṛd upastīrya dvir dadhi dvir abhighārayet
udvāsanavelāyām āmikṣayoḥ kharjūrasaktūn āvapataḥ
mārutyāṃ pratiprasthātā meṣam avadadhāti vāruṇyām adhvaryur meṣīm
āsādayantau vipariharataḥ
vāruṇīniṣkāṣaṃ nidadhāti
uttarasminn agnau saṃmṛṣṭe 'saṃmṛṣṭe dakṣiṇasmin pratiprasthātā patnīṃ pṛcchati katibhir mithunam acara iti
satyaṃ vivācayiṣet
yān nirdiśet tān varuṇo gṛhṇātv iti brūyāt
praghāsyān havāmaha iti karambhapātrāṇy ādāya yajamānaḥ patnī cāpareṇa vihāram anuparikramya purastāt pratyañcau tiṣṭhantau śirasy ādhāya dakṣiṇasminn agnau śūrpeṇa juhutaḥ
mo ṣū ṇa iti yajamānaḥ puronuvākyāṃ japati
yad grāma ity ubhau yājyāṃ nigadya juhutaḥ
akran karmeti vyutkrāmantāv anumantrayete
adhvaryur vā juhuyād anvārabheyātām etau
ājyabhāgābhyāṃ pracarya srukpāṇiḥ pratiprasthātākāṅkṣati yāvad adhvaryur aindrāgnaṣaṣṭhaiḥ pracarati
mārutyāḥ pratiprasthātā pūrveṇāvadānena saha meṣīm avadyati vāruṇyā adhvaryur uttareṇa saha meṣam
iḍāvatsarīyāṃ svastim āśāsa iti yajamāno japati
mithunau gāvau dakṣiṇā
samavanīya vājinaṃ bhakṣayaty upāste pratiprasthātā
patnīsaṃyājān samiṣṭayajur adhvaryur juhoti yathā paśubandhe
tūṣṇīṃ pratiprasthātā srucaṃ vikṣārayati
vāruṇīniṣkāṣeṇa tuṣaiś cāvabhṛthaṃ yanti yathā some sāma ṛjīṣabhakṣaṇaṃ snānam iti parihāpya
nivartayate

agnis tigmeneti samānam

agnaye 'nīkavate prātar aṣṭākapālo marudbhyaḥ sāṃtapanebhyo madhyandine carur marudbhyo gṛhamedhebhyaḥ sarvāsāṃ dugdhe sāyam odana indrasya niṣkāṣaḥ
yajuṣā vatsān apākaroti
apavitre dohayati
nedhmābarhiḥ saṃnahyati
nopabhṛtyājyaṃ gṛhṇāti
odanasya śaroniṣkāṣaṃ nidadhāti

na sāmidhenīr anvāha

savatsā gāvo vasanti
prācīnarātre 'bhivānyāyā agnihotryāś ca vatsau badhnanti
purā prātar agnihotrād gārhapatye śaroniṣkāṣapūrṇāṃ darvīṃ parāpatety ṛṣabham āhvayate
yad ṛṣabho na rūyād brahmā brūyāj juhudhīti
marudbhyaḥ krīḍibhyaḥ sākaṃ raśmibhiḥ saptakapālaṃ nirvapet pracared vā
mahāhaviṣā yajate sottaravedim agniṃ praṇīya

sa āhavanīyaḥ

agreṇa nityam āhavanīyam atihāraḥ

tūṣṇīkāṃs tryambakān puroḍāśān ekakapālān pratipuruṣaṃ yajamānasyaikādhikān

śalākāsthaṃ manthaṃ karoti

agnaye devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
